Know thyself is the quintessence.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">It has no founder or a Supreme head. There is NO supreme middleman like the Pope who can canonise a human into a saint, by giving bullshit, to the unsuspecting masses.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">It is a movement based on principles or evolved over time code of &nbsp;Dharma. It is a relentless pursuit of truth, flexible to suit all situations.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Hinduism does NOT care for individual leadership or hierarchy.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">I have never said a prayer in my life--even when my ship was 38 miles off the eye of a Category 5 storm.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">(Read my post SUPER TYPHOON BART, THE PERFECT STORM dated 22nd Dec 2010).</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Who knows , tomorrow, I may be less cocky of my own abilities and could start praying fervently for deliverance.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">This is the wonder of Hinduism. I don't care to visit temples, I don't care to pray, yet--I am a believing and practising Hindu.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Hinduism is the world's oldest religion 11000 years old, when the white man's land was under the quaternary ice age sheets.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Yet, <span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue;\">Hinduism is NOT a religion. It is a way of life</span>.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue;\">This is a religion without fundamentals or lack of compulsions.</span>&nbsp;You cannot get ex-communicated for NOT toeing the line.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">This is why India has never attacked any other country in the past history, but has been invaded again and again and again. If every Indian had picked up a stone like the Palestinians , we could have driven away the invaders long back or killed them like mad jackals on the school street, in one day, ages ago.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">It is a faith so unique, that it gives space for every other religion. Hinduism has never claimed to be the only true religion.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Hinduism has never converted , by guile ( Christian missionaries ) or force ( Muslim ) -- nor has a army of missionaries , ramming it down unwilling throats.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">I feel happy as a Hindu to meet people of other faiths, and converse with them, without being burdened by the conviction , that my religion is the best, and i have embarked on the right path, that every one else has missed.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Of my top 3 friends, one is Muslim, One is Roman Catholic, and one is Hindu. Both my children studied in Muslim majority school Hilltop School , Calicut for 12 years from LKG. &nbsp;The ratio of seats for Muslims is 90%-- as the school it is run by a Muslim trust. What you believe in we do to our children , right? My elder son was adjudged the best student of this Muslim school , the year he passed out. &nbsp;So, is there any discrimination? &nbsp;This school was so orthodox that on Friday , they took Muslim children to the mosque by bus.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Though we use the Bhagawat Gita to swear an oath, as set down by our British rulers in court--we do NOT have a single holy book, like the Bible or Koran. Such has been the tolerance to deviant beliefs.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">I am proud of the diversity, the range, and the lofty metaphysical aspirations of Vedanta.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">The eternal truths in the Vedas were written by our great seers without junk DNA in their bodies and king sized resonating pineal glands. It is NOT mere speculation of guesswork.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">At the heart of Hinduism remains mans' essential quest for union with the Absolute supreme.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Hinduism is based on reason and NOT faith--unless the faith is an extension of reason. It has its won beliefs, timeless traditions, ethics, rituals, philosophy and theology.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-y00eSZvR-wc/TV6thoR-gmI/AAAAAAAADgA/Wg6IikUhkN0/s1600/images+%25285%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-l3ifPgvX6Vo/TV9NQQn6a9I/AAAAAAAADg4/_4AAi8LW_SM/s1600/images+%252810%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><b>The Bhagavad-Gita</b>&nbsp;( discourse just before the Mahabharata war in 4000 BC , from Charioteer Lord Krishna to Prince Arjuna ) conveys the essence of Hinduism as follows--</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><i>He who hates no single being, is friendly and compassionate, free from self-regard and vanity, patient, contented, fixed on me in heart and mind, is dear to me.</i><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto;\">\n<i><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></i></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><i>Hell has three gates: lust, anger, and greed.</i><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto;\">\n<i><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></i></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><i>There has never been a time when you and I have not existed, nor will there be a time when we will cease to exist. As the same person inhabits the body through childhood, youth, and old age, so too at the time of death he attains another body. The wise are not deluded by these changes.</i><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto;\">\n<i><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></i></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><i>He who is full of faith and zeal, and has subdued his senses attains knowledge; having attained knowledge, he soon attains supreme peace.</i><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<i><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Do your duty. Sieze the moment. The time to do, is NOW.&nbsp;</span></i><br />\n<i><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></i><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-OAsY16BJ2YE/TV6tx1M5JTI/AAAAAAAADgE/MIrdRg_6wnY/s1600/images+%25284%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-OAsY16BJ2YE/TV6tx1M5JTI/AAAAAAAADgE/MIrdRg_6wnY/s1600/images+%25284%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 15pt; margin: 7.5pt 0in 15pt; vertical-align: baseline;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">The popularly recited Hindu invocation demonstrates this concern for universal kinship:<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div align=\"center\" class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 15pt; margin: 7.5pt 0in 15pt; text-align: center; vertical-align: baseline;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><i>Om sarve bhavantu sukhinah. Sarve santu niraamayaah.<br />\nSarve bhadraani pashyantu. Maa kaschid dukhbhaag bhavet.<br />\n<br />\nMay all beings be happy. May all beings be healthy.<br />\nMay all beings experience prosperity. May none in the world suffer.</i><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"line-height: 20px;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">The unadulterated pluralism is captured in the ancient Sanskrit hymn:</span></span><br />\n<br />\n<div align=\"center\" class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 15pt; margin: 7.5pt 0in 15pt; text-align: center; vertical-align: baseline;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><i>Ekam sat vipraha bahudha vadanti<br />\nTruth is one, the wise call it by many names.</i><o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><i><br />\n</i></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-LRTW3JgL2jE/TV6t2o2ukbI/AAAAAAAADgI/BROJvkNuyGc/s1600/images+%25287%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-LRTW3JgL2jE/TV6t2o2ukbI/AAAAAAAADgI/BROJvkNuyGc/s1600/images+%25287%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div align=\"center\" class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 15pt; margin: 7.5pt 0in 15pt; text-align: center; vertical-align: baseline;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><i><br />\n</i></span></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">The Vedas evolved in 7000 BC, but was penned down in 5000 BC, on the banks of the Saraswati. It is NOT a set of preconceived ideas.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">The fundamental deities are Brahma, Vishnu and Shiva. ( Creator/ preserver/ destroyer ) or Tamas/ Sattva Rajas &nbsp;of the Yin Yang trident.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Ancient India has survived over 12000 years, because Hinduism was developed along Spiritual lines, NOT materialistic lines.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Hinduism is a living organism-- a vest tree with countless branches.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"apple-style-span\"><span style=\"line-height: 115%;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Most Hindus believe in the doctrine of reincarnation. This is the belief that each of us has a soul and that our souls are involved in a cycle of birth, death and rebirth.&nbsp;</span></span></span><br />\n<span class=\"apple-style-span\"><span style=\"line-height: 115%;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></span></span><br />\n<span class=\"apple-style-span\"><span style=\"line-height: 115%;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Reincarnation is tied closely to the doctrine of karma. <span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue;\">Karma is the belief that the actions during the previous life determine the conditions of each person's birth.&nbsp;</span></span></span></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Here is what a few people said of Hinduism, after understanding this religion that has NOT reduced itself to one man, one book, one faith.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/-k32OaOkocTc/TW5dKNPeflI/AAAAAAAAD2c/fgDgK_EvRRs/s1600/images+%25283%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/-k32OaOkocTc/TW5dKNPeflI/AAAAAAAAD2c/fgDgK_EvRRs/s1600/images+%25283%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 24px;\"><span style=\"color: blue;\"><b>Dr. Carl Sagan:&nbsp;</b><em><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"line-height: 14px;\">The Hindu religion is the only one of the world's great faiths dedicated to the idea that the Cosmos itself undergoes an immense, indeed an infinite, number of deaths and rebirths. &nbsp;</span><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"line-height: 14px;\">It is the only religion in which the time scales correspond, to those of modern scientific cosmology<b>.&nbsp;</b></span><span style=\"line-height: 115%;\"><b>T</b></span><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"line-height: 14px;\">he most elegant and sublime of these is a representation of the creation of the universe at the beginning of each cosmic cycle, a motif known as&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;; font-stretch: normal; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; line-height: normal;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\">&nbsp;</span></span></em></span></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 24px;\"><span style=\"color: blue;\"><em><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;; font-stretch: normal; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; line-height: normal;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\">T</span><span class=\"Apple-style-span\">he dance of Shiva</span><span class=\"Apple-style-span\">.</span> &nbsp;</span>In the upper right hand is a drum whose sound is the sound of creation. In the upper left hand is a tongue of flame, a reminder that the universe, now newly created, with billions of years from now will be utterly destroyed.</em></span></span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 18pt; margin-bottom: 1.2pt; margin-left: 0.5in; mso-list: l0 level2 lfo1; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; tab-stops: list 1.0in; text-indent: -0.25in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 18pt; margin: 4.8pt 0in 6pt;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><i><b>Mark Twain:&nbsp;</b><b>&nbsp;\"</b>Land of religions, cradle of human race, birthplace of human speech, grandmother of legend, great grandmother of tradition. The land that all men desire to see and having seen once even by a glimpse, would not give that glimpse for the shows of the rest of the globe combined.\"<o:p></o:p></i></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue; line-height: 24px;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\"><span style=\"color: black;\"><span style=\"mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">Hindus&nbsp;themselves&nbsp;prefer to use the Sanskrit term <span style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: italic;\"><span style=\"color: blue;\">sanatana dharma</span> </span>for their religious tradition. <span style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: italic;\">Sanatana </span>as \u201ceternal moral order\u201d</span><span style=\"mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\"> </span><span style=\"mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">encourages Hindus to seek s and moral truth wherever it might be found, each individual must realize this truth through his or her own systematic effort.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span></span></span></span></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 24px;\"></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 24px;\"></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 24px;\"></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 24px;\"></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 24px;\"></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 24px;\"></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 24px;\"></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 24px;\"></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 24px;\"></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 24px;\"></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 24px;\"></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 24px;\"></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 24px;\"></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 24px;\"></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 24px;\"></span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 24px;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\"><span style=\"color: black;\"><span style=\"mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">Hindu scripture, based on the insights of Hindu sages and seers, serves primarily as a guidebook. But ultimately truth comes to us through direct consciousness of the divine or the ultimate reality. as GOD. Hindus refer to it as Brahman.. (This is not to be confused with <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Brahmin meaning priest.)</span><span style=\"mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\"> </span><span style=\"mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\"></span></span></span></span></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 24px;\">\n</span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 24px;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\"><span style=\"color: black;\"><span style=\"mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">In&nbsp;many&nbsp;religions&nbsp;truth is delivered or revealed from a divine source and enters the world through a single agent: for example, Abraham in Judaism, Jesus Christ in Christianity, and Muhammad in Islam. These truths are then recorded in scriptures that serve as a source of knowledge of divine wisdom: the Hebrew Bible, the New Testament of the Christian Bible, and the Koran. In the Hindu tradition, by contrast, there is no single revelation) by which people may achieve knowledge of the divine or lead a life backed by religious law. </span></span></span></span></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 24px;\">\n</span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 24px;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\"><span style=\"color: black;\"><span style=\"mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">The Hindu tradition acknowledges that there are many paths by which people may seek and experience religious understanding and direction. It also claims that every individual has the potential to achieve enlightenment.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>. </span></span></span></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 24px;\"><br /></span>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 24px;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\"><span style=\"color: black;\"><span style=\"mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">Hinduism\u2019s universal world-view and its willingness to accept and celebrate diverse philosophies, deities, symbols, and practices, makes it a religion that emphasizes similarities and shared characteristics rather than differences.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></span></span></span></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 24px;\">\n</span>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 24px;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\"><span style=\"color: black;\"><span style=\"mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>The Hindu tradition , unlike other religions --has always concerned itself with the human situation rather than the Hindu situation. Instead of basing its identity on separating Hindu from non-Hindu or believer from non-believer, Hinduism has sought to recognize principles and practices that would lead any individual to become a better human being and understand and live in harmony with dharma.</span><span style=\"mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\"> </span></span></span></span></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 24px;\">\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\"><span style=\"color: black;\"><span style=\"mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\"></span><span style=\"mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">The&nbsp;distinction&nbsp;of&nbsp;dharma from the Western sense of religion is crucial to understanding Hindu religious identity<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>Dharma&nbsp;is&nbsp;an&nbsp;all-important concept for Hindus. In addition to tradition and moral order, it also signifies the path of knowledge and correct action. </span></span></span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\"><span style=\"color: black;\"><span style=\"mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">Because of Hinduism\u2019s emphasis on living in accordance with dharma, anyone who is striving for spiritual knowledge and seeking the right course of ethical action is, in the broadest sense, a follower of <span style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: italic;\">sanatana dharma</span>.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></div>\n<span style=\"color: black;\">&nbsp; </span> <div style=\"line-height: 115%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , &quot;sans-serif&quot;; line-height: 115%;\"><span style=\"color: black;\">The chain of births and deaths\u2014is called samsara.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<span style=\"color: black;\">  </span><br />\n<div style=\"line-height: 115%;\">\n<span style=\"color: black;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , &quot;sans-serif&quot;; line-height: 115%;\">Samsara</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , &quot;sans-serif&quot;; line-height: 115%;\">&nbsp;is&nbsp;caused&nbsp;by&nbsp;a lack of knowledge of our true self and our resultant desire for fulfilment outside ourselves. We continue to embody ourselves, or be reborn, in this infinite and eternal universe as a result of these unfulfilled desires. </span></span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"color: black;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , &quot;sans-serif&quot;; line-height: 115%;\">The chain of births lets us resume the pursuit. The law that governs <span style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: italic;\">samsara</span> is called karma. Each birth and death we undergo is determined by the balance sheet of our <span style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: italic;\">karma</span>\u2014that is, in accordance with the actions performed and the dispositions acquired in the past.</span></span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 115%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 115%;\">\n<span style=\"color: black;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , &quot;sans-serif&quot;; line-height: 115%;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: italic;\">&nbsp;Karma</span>&nbsp;is&nbsp;a&nbsp;crucial&nbsp;Hindu concept. According to the doctrine of <span style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: italic;\">karma</span>, our present condition in life is the consequence of the actions of our previous lives. The choices we have made in the past directly affect our condition in this life, and the choices we make today and thereafter will have consequences for our future lives in <span style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: italic;\">samsara</span>. </span></span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"color: black;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , &quot;sans-serif&quot;; line-height: 115%;\">An understanding of this interconnection, according to Hindu teachings, can lead an individual towards right choices, deeds, thoughts, and desires, without the need for an external set of commandments. Under the doctrine of <span style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: italic;\">karma</span>, the ability to make choices remains with the individual.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<span style=\"color: black;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;\"><span style=\"color: black;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\">The sacred fire serves as a witness to the vows exchanged between the bride and the bridegroom. />\n<br />\n1)home grown TML centrifuge tests ( STRANGE new concept those days )<br />\nwere done with representative samples from barges -- before loading. <br />\n<br />\nrepresentative because solid ore pile is NOT liquid cargo, where you can<br />\nshove a UTI sampler in between --so a SHARP SS METAL PIPE IS USED TO<br />\nINVADE INTO THE MIDDLE OF THE ORE PILE -- AND EXTRACT-- like a pipette<br />\nin a chemical lab.<br />\n<br />\n2)no working allowed in rain ( to force the barges and shore pile to<br />\ncover up )<br />\n<br />\n3)3 cm radar was used for rain prognosis.<br for i have learnt<br />\nquantum physics , just to author a book on life beyond 5 human senses )<br />\n-- but still ore and water will fall within the scope of newtons 3rd law<br />\n--<br />\n<br />\nit states that for every action there is a equal and opposite reaction.<br />\nso whether you kick the hammer or hit the hammer on your foot -- the<br />\neffect is pretty much the same --<br />\n<br />\nso with the every beat of the deadly IMSBC metal can -- water flows past<br />\nore-- and vice versa -- where F effective minus F friction = MA<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" />\nrepresentative sample extract from the innards of the SS metal pipe, is<br />\nshoved into a FINE SS mesh sock and sealed.<br />\n<br />\nthe transparent glass bottle is now put inside a metal can with a handle<br />\n-- a rope is attached to the handle and the whole paraphernalia rotated<br />\naround the head ( like how a old sailor of yore swung the lead , before<br />\nthe throw ) .<br />\n<br />\n-- water gets centrifuged like how the laundry spinner centrifuges water<br />\noff the wet clothes. &nbsp;water which comes out of ore inside the mesh sock <br />\n-- is on ONE WAY \"ACTION\" LANE , for the mesh acts as hundred non-return<br />\nvalves -- <br />\n<br />\nwater accumulates inside the glass bottle and it can be seen from<br />\noutside -- it is then quantified and photographed --<br />\n<br />\nthe longer the radius of the rope the greater the centrifuge force.<br />\n<br />\nancient indians extracted water from milk this way ( panchatantra tales<br />\n) 7000 150%;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-GNYA2TQ9JxA/TV3q_1T3yqI/AAAAAAAADfI/Xg2bJ3DI3l4/s1600/images+%25281%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Recommended procedures for testing fine ores or bulk cargoes which may liquify is covered in Appendix D1 of the Code.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Many ores which are essentially insoluble in water and which contain mainly finely divided material, may liquefy on ocean voyages if they contain an excessive amount of water when loaded or if they subsequently become wetted. This applies even though they may appear to be in the form of dry powders of granular materials.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Such liquefaction is basically due to energy being applied to the cargo. This can be as a result ROLLING AT SEA. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\"><br />\n</span></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Liquefaction must be monitored during the voyage if the load port stock pile was wet. Any cargo of finely divided material which tends to flatten and which develops a putty-like surface during a voyage, has started to liquefy.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The ship should take urgent action and should proceed to the nearest port of refuge, after altering course/ speed to avoid rolling/ pitching \u2014even if this means you have to go to a farther port of refuge.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">A list of cargoes known to liquefy is given in Appendix A of the IMO BC Code, but this list is not exhaustive. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Master must insist upon a written statement from the shippers or charterers confirming that the product concerned will not liquefy if it contains an excess of moisture.&nbsp;</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Saving life is Master\u2019s duty.&nbsp;</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The Insurance companies are more worried about moolah.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">A certificate should be provided stating the TML for the cargo is a must for wet concentrates. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Master must examine stockpiles of cargoes before loading. Water oozing from such stockpiles is an indication that <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>the stockpile has a moisture content above the TML. Any obviously wet material should be rejected as such cargo might form a shear plane on which a dry cargo loaded subsequently, might slide around.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">If masters are doubtful about the condition of a cargo, they can read the can test <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>described in the IMO BC Code, Section 8.3 at Page 24. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span>Samples must be drawn from lower level of the pile .<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">When loading at freezing temperatures , check for inherent dry ice crystals, which can melt later inside ship\u2019s hold.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Samples are drawn from various levels including the bottoms of piles and that these are warmed and then tested by the can test.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><br />\n</div><br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; />\n</span></i><br />\n<i><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue;\">The following is an actual &nbsp;PRE-DELIVERY OBSERVATION LIST, &nbsp;I made as a Delivery Master, for a highly automated, ( full of PLC and microprocessors ) &nbsp;brand new Chemical tanker, made to Euro Standards, in a reputed European Yard.</span></i><br />\n<i><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue;\"><br />\n</span></i><br />\n<i><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue;\">After the delivery was made , i suggested to the Owners and Managers, that we must sell off the substandard ship, which will be a nightmare to run.</span></i><br />\n<i><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue;\"><br />\n</span></i><br />\n<i><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue;\">--and strongly advised them that the subsequent 7 sister ships must not have the same moronic mistakes-- dumped on ship by feckless Yard, Class, Makers etc etc.</span></i><br />\n<i><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue;\"><br />\n</span></i><br />\n<i><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: red;\">After all what is the use of a Chemical tanker which has----- 600 SS lugs with 2 holes in all the cargo tanks-- whose Emg fire pump cant take suction at sea ( or in port in Ballast draft )------ with WORLD RECORD blind sectors in radar displays!.</span></i><br />\n<i><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue;\"><br />\n</span></i><br />\n<i><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue;\">WARNING: DO NOT TRY TO READ MORE THAN 50 ITEMS IN ONE SITTING, LEST YOUR GREY MATTER OVERHEATS.</span></i><br />\n<i><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue;\"><br />\n</span></i><br />\n<i><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue;\">Actually the list ran to nearly 900 items. A lot of deficiencies were done up on the personal initiative of the NO 1 boss of the yard , who was a strong man and was very resourceful. I had a one on one equation with him.&nbsp;</span></i><br />\n<i><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue;\"><br />\n</span></i><br />\n<i><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue;\">This is a warning to all Chemical Masters and Chief engineers--dont expect the Class and the Makers and the Yard, to know what it takes to run a good chemical tanker safely. &nbsp;The ignorance is just mindboggling.</span></i><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-IE-QKWzHbNM/TnciFFxpivI/AAAAAAAAGSM/BYC8XOM3CQc/s1600/ndw.gif\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-IE-QKWzHbNM/TnciFFxpivI/AAAAAAAAGSM/BYC8XOM3CQc/s1600/ndw.gif\" /></a></div>\n<i><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue;\"><br />\n</span></i><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; color: red;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<b><span style=\"background-color: yellow; line-height: 150%;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: red; font-size: large;\">XXXXX \u2013&nbsp;&nbsp; CHEMICAL TANKER PRE-DELIVERY OBSERVATIONS<o:p></o:p></span></span></b><br />\n<b><span style=\"background-color: yellow; line-height: 150%;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: red; font-size: large;\"><br /></span></span></b></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-ZTGXoHFAu8E/UgtiFVSZr7I/AAAAAAAAlKA/E0-3nGR9jlU/s1600/images.jpgoiung6tr.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"265\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-ZTGXoHFAu8E/UgtiFVSZr7I/AAAAAAAAlKA/E0-3nGR9jlU/s400/images.jpgoiung6tr.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">1)The Framo drain tank vent to which the HPU overflow is connected&nbsp; is exposed to sea spray\u2014must be recessed indoors, and that too with an air filter. ( yard supply tank interfacing ). <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">2)The ensign flag staff welded on to the free fall LBoat davit&nbsp; , must be cropped and relocated\u2014or the boat gets damaged when retrieving.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">3)The forward tow cable chain enclosing must be lined from inside with Teflon tapes, or galvanic corrosion will destroy the casing steel within 2 years. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">4)All hydraulic connectors of cranes ,.free fall LB,&nbsp; winches, entire deck valve hydraulics connectors and penetration points&nbsp; must be denso taped.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">5)Shelves in fore peak store and pump mans mid ship store are fast assembly type light duty, the type used in shore offices which cannot with stand the rigours of stormy seas. The horizontal parts shelves are steel without friction coefficient.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">6)Free fall Lboat external aft drain is choked\u2014the battery hydrogen release vent is blocked \u2013explosion <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">7)All the existing mooring ropes ( yard ) are reeved wrong on the drums\u2014this causes undue strain on the steel structure. Note the maker is Rolls Royce and brakes are hydraulic.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">8)A 3 cm sharp rake bar is fitted on the bulbous bow. The after most part must be cropped by one metre on the next TBN build, as it has split the drydock block wood cap underneath. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">9)Holes must be punched on the winch platform platings, to prevent getting adrift in green seas.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">10)There are 2 high heeling tanks of 675 cum at shipside\u2014it has lost its meaning as it is connected to the common line. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">11) There is a huge void tank about 1/3 of the FP tank , on top of the forepeak tank. It is a ideal place for a tank cleaning FW tank, as a press up expansion tank to the low TCFW DB tank.\u2014all it requires is a pipeline. For a ship of this size and epoxy/ zinc lining , 557 tons of TCFW is grossly insufficient\u2014any chemical man will vouch for this..<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">12)There is no provision in the plans for a hose cradle ( on a chemical tanker!)<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">13)The forward cargo tanks deck delivery pipes&nbsp; should be fitted with a drain cock at the manifold where they rise up to meet the high level manifold.\u2014or some cargo always remains there. Useful for deslopping pipelines. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">14)There is no galley AC\u2014as all new build chemical tankers have. There is a provision\u2014but it has been wrongly connected to the steam connection instead of the evaporator side. I am sure galley with all its hot plates , requires no heating. The cook is going to roast\u2014to prevent this the galley door has to be kept open, so that the accommodation AC can cool galley, with the high capacity galley exhaust running. This will cause vacuum in accommodation at terminal.\u2014something which is absolutely not desired.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">15)There is&nbsp; Furuno Loran\u2014it is not working at present, as the world coverage area is limited. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">16)At XXX dry dock with nil list and declivity of blocks aft trim\u2014after a rainfall there is tons ( at least 8 tons ) of water collected in accommodation decks which will enter working shoes of agent , customs or coast guard \u2014as there is NIL camber, and dented plate pockets .On most ships the accumulation is just a few litres. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">17)There is no UTI tube perforated extension fitted in cargo tanks. This will be a deficiency as the ship will be carrying static cargoes.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">18)The Framo deck mounted heater , always&nbsp; has a provision to have bottom to top recirc.\u2014which splashes on the bulkhead and flows down.&nbsp; Here it is bottom to bottom\u2014take the cargo sediment from the bottom and put is back at the same level. There are&nbsp; no recirc nozzles to remove cargo sediment from the bottom. Squeegeeing efforts will be a night mare.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">19)There are no recir nozzles fitted for cargo drops.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">20)The slop tanks 10W have HO storage tanks adjacent. Adjacent heat of 45C ( and greater )&nbsp; in addition to preventing cargo from being loaded due to incompatibility can also cause ocean loss due to evaporation. After a few years bacteria will chomp off the steel and create a hole . Ever noticed that ships always got prematurely scrapped due to WBT sections 10 inches off heated HO bulkheads , getting corroded?<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">21)The incinerator has been installed next to the poop deck garbage bins\u2014so convenient\u2014but it is next to the foam tank \u2013and foam is going to be caked soon due to heat. Consider that the incinerator runs 10 hours a day minimum, burning HO sludge. A silver heat shield must protect the tank.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">22)The zinc silicate lining of cargo tanks, XXX is not a good effort. No prizes for anybody who guesses that it is a maiden attempt , by the yard. The spray painting is not done in a uniform fashion causing high DFT at overlap areas. Plenty of finishing touches have been done with paint brush which is never done, as the high DFT thickness of around 200 microns will cause the inorganic zinc to shed into the cargo and cause horrendous contamination claims. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">23)The electrical bonding to prevent static electricity explosions is very poor \u2013all over the ship.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">24)It is usual for porous aDsorbent zinc silicate tank ships to have a Methanol deck tank to store this tank cleaning chemical.\u2014and also a DI water set. We do not have both.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">25)The epoxy cargo tanks have bright yellow paint patches\u2014especially the tank domes and butterworth ports. Only 2 coats of 150 microns \u2013first Pastel red and second light grey was applied. While all are eager to say it is UV damage\u2014it is plainly evident that the unsolicited 3<sup>rd</sup> coat of touch up paint was different.\u2014yellow colour has&nbsp; to do more with the ageing pot life of the paint used and humidity control , after the first 2 coats.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">26)Every cargo tank has more than 500 plate lug eyes&nbsp; ( 2 holes ) and ring eyes welded for tank staging. This exists on both sides and ceiling.&nbsp; A chemical tanker carries high melting point cargoes. Tankcleaning will be a clingage nightmare after say Palm oil in cold weather. Also some of these plate eyes are blocking the smooth passage of UTI tubes and sampling point. They will also damage these sensitive equipment or cause static electricity sparks. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">27) There is no mist box inside the funnel.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">28) The Email is not planned to be in masters cabin\u2014to make his life easier. It is not right for the master to go on the bridge and disturb the OOW.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">29)There is no reinforcement plate at the sharp anchor flukes.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">30)Panama shelter is required on bridge wings, as ship is broad. There is a provision for putting sockets\u2014if used the shelter will be just too large ( 4 times&nbsp; the size ) and unwieldy and will blow off with the wind, as many ships have learnt the hard way.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">31)There is no proper water extraction facility for the HO sludge prior putting into the incinerator. This will cause sputtering and extinguishing of flame. And whatever is extracted goes back to square one. Smooth incineration is a must or man hours are wasted.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">32)All toilets have both the bottom drains ( shower/ WC ) forward part of the ship. This means when the ship has a stern trim , the filthy water remains there on the white tiles&nbsp; \u2013at least 3 inches. This will become a PSC deficiency\u2014Vermin and lack of hygiene in toilets is frowned on by all PSC memorandums. THE CAMBER TO THE SCUPPERS MUST BE REDONE PRIOR DELIVERY.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">33) Cargo tank PV valve orifice is on deck plating\u2014this is wrong , it must be in the tank dome above the level of deck plate. With a trim in heavy pitching , cargo from forward will enter the PV pipes.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">34)There must be a provision to lash down the crane boom in addition to tightening the runner wire\u2014for hurricane weather.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">35)The HL/ OF alarm testing knob is beneath the deck longitudinal frames\u2014in rough seas these knobs will be submerged. If a alarm does not work, it becomes a deficiency for everybody\u2014with some terminals even banning cargo work , in California.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">36)There is no lashing arrangement for both sides gangways\u2014at least 3 are required along its length as it is situated on the main deck.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">37)Only 5 phones have zero call public address facility. It is better that all phones have it as a contingency measure for ISPS.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">38)The not so rigid PV valve stack platform vibrates\u2014loss of nitrogen pad. -<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">39)The HL/ OF alarm protrusion which is a static electricity dischg point must either be earthed or have a Teflon suppressor. If not the class must state that the type approval for earthing is considered..<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">40)The ballast pumps are located inside the ballast tanks to save on an aft pumproom, which is perfectly OK. . But to expect pumps at 3 wings to take uphill suction from 7 wings through a huge diameter suction pipeline is wishful thinking\u2014as the air will skim from top uphill and liquid will keep sliding back down hill. Imagine sipping from a glass with a high diameter straw. Cavitation during ballast exchange due to bubbles from forward bow wave and pounding will scour away the pump casing. On the next ships in the series, the sea chests must be aft of midships. Ballast ROB is sure in aft tanks unless we fit stripping lines of small dia. Ballast ROB means cargo sacrifice.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">41)Whichever cabins have the bed lamps to the aft side of ship\u2014they must be relocated forward.\u2014or all will get a rush of blood into their brains, due to trim.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">42)A fortune has been spent for UMS , bridge manoevering and automation, but there is no data logger\u2014this means manual telegraph bell book entries. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">43)The 2 chairs on the bridge and not approved for pilot. Swinging unstable chairs, with no arm rests.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">44)The steering gear vent is an exhaust vent. It must be reversed, by shifting a phase lead&nbsp; wire.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">45)Framo insists on NIL pipelines on top of the cargo pumps, as a blocked cofferdam or leak at pump head will entail lifting up the whole pump stack with a crane. Here all the stbd side tanks have&nbsp; 3 layers of pipelines immediately on top of the pumps.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">46)The Framo cargo pump delivery valve is located very far away from the pump. This means after blowing the stack at least 1600 litres of cargo will drop back downhill in tanks aft of manifold. Here the manifold is on top of the cargo pipes and the aft tanks are not tilted towards the manifold, instead they are parallel to the deck. The huge unpumpable quantity requires , superstripping to be done with the small dia pipeline, which is usually not necessary as the cargo surveyor accepts low ROB.&nbsp; This super stripping will take a very long time.\u2014many hours of delay at each disport\u2014loss of company reputation&nbsp; <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">47)There are many vibration spots which needs to be stiffened. The EPIRB perch on stbd bridge wing is one. Both bridge wings jump up and down. Dep port will have squat induced vibrations.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">48)The AIS fitted in June 2007, has Category ABCD of Marpol mentioned. We are paying money for XYZ--&nbsp; not ABCD which got booted off last new year eve.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">49)The anemometer is a new design without a wind vane which is usually used by all on main deck for finding the wind direction with carcinogenic and poisonous cargoes. A wind sock must be provided for berth use.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">50)The radar blind sectors ( excessive- world record ) must be posted on the wheel house at radar site by the yard. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">51)Yard must provide a squat table , for various sinkage levels in the wheelhouse for display. OR the UTI tube must be relocated at aft bulkhead.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">87)All deck mounted heaters are low capacity. The must be vents for both heavy and light vapours.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">89)The ER ODMCS must have a spare dessicator cartridge.
