All fire extinguishers must be colour coded with bands in IMO format.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">96)There is no provision for letting free air into the tanks , while dischg high MP cargoes -\u2013as there are no flame arrested purge pipes. Most chemicals do not require IG or N2 padding , some shippers do not want nitrogen. Oxygen dependent inhibitors are used for most polymerizing cargoes like Styrene Monomer.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">97) Sewage treatment plant \u201c holding tank\u201d&nbsp; stiffeners are inside the tank, not outside.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">98)During the pre-sea trial crash astern test it was noticed that\u2014after giving a stern kick&nbsp;&nbsp; the first kick astern comes at 25 rpm\u2014this means the first air brake and cam falling astern came here. Ideally the air brake should happen at around 35 rpm. This saves a crucial 2 minutes which is the time for a ship with forward momemtum to come from 35 rpm to 25 rpm ( with engines stopped ).&nbsp; It was noticed that the air bottles were almost full when the engines responded astern. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">99)There is a huge steam return inspection chamber aft of slops. All steam return lines from deck heaters have individual glass ports and cascades. Initial water which has to be wasted ( as the ship gets old , the quantity gets more ) is wasted on deck, which is not possible in most terminals , it can be done only at sea. There must be a provision to lead it to the drain tank .<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">100) 3 pronged spider/ octopus for chemical recirc in tanks must be provided to fit the orifice downstream of the delivery block valve.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">101) Usually the freefall LB cannot be entered unless the tying down arrangement of the boat&nbsp; to the cradle rail is released---the senhouse slip wire is attached to the LB door, when released the safety clamps fall off by gravity. . Here there is a battening down hook type arrangement , but if anybody forgets to open it , the LB will be in a dangerous position. There must be an interlock from this hook release to the LB door.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">102)Foam tank sounding pipe is too low and water can ingress if any scupper is choked. The sounding rod does not have any calibration.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">103)Testing of HL/ OF alarm requires some expertise as it is a single shaft which has to be pulled up. If it is pulled up too fast the OF alarm comes.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">104)The HL/OF alarm mounted on the bridge front bulkhead is an air operated siren. In cold weather it may not work\u2014it should have been a simple electric alarm. We all know the pitfalls of an air whistle in freezing weather. This air whistle is too loud and shrill, and no watch keeper will be rested.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">105)The deck pipeline configuration is not a professional one. The operational aspect has been ignored. Carrying high melting point cargoes in winter will be a nightmare, as there are many areas where the cargo will get frozen in pipelines, including small stripping lines. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">106)The framo drain tank vent is fitted with a wire mesh\u2014it is meant to be an air filter of 12 microns.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">107)The framo stack purging air cock and the stripping manual valve upstream of the delivery valve is too widely separated, by four bays of high walls. Manual stripping has to be done on chemical tankers. Bays must be made more accessible by installing vertical ladders and steps with vaulting handles. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">108)The foam pump non return delivery valve is located in the wrong place. It must be re-installed towards the pump , down stream of the recirc line.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">109)The steam inlet to deck must have a main blank and individual blanks before deck mounted heaters.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">110)We have paid money for a rescue boat, not for a dinghy where there are only 2 seats\u2014the rest must squat on the floor , in a ungainly and impossible fashion\u2014with nothing to hold on to.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">111)The entire exterior hull of this new ship looks like the ribs of a starving horse\u2014with frames sticking out in a sore fashion. Having taken delivery of quite a few new chemical tankers\u2014I can say , this is not normal.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">112)There is no tank cleaning chemical dosing tank.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">113) The funnel top does not have a sloping arrangement , only two drains are located aft. In even keel conditions the water will slosh around.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">114) There are no eyes on funnel top for painting the funnel in future using stages and rope.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">115)All cargo tank butterworth ports have only single hard packing and there are only 3 butterfly nuts keeping the lid shut. As you know even in Panama canal , the inspectors look for gas leaking from BW ports\u2014and delay transit if not rectifies. Chemical tankers require double defence packing and the hinge is not considered as a tightening arrangement.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">116)Since the 23 capacity accommodation was swarming with nearly 100 personnel during many days of sea trials \u2013all toilets , cabins, public spaces etc are filthy\u2014with no daily cleaning. The ship must be delivered in a clean condition.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">117)The incinerator refractory must have a guarantee certificate. Incinerator will be working 12 hours every day.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">118)The AE funnel stacks smoke during low&nbsp; load conditions\u2014this is in a brand new condition with good grade gas oil.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">119)The fire wires on reels ford and aft must be vinyl coated to last longer and for safe handling.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">120)The ME HO fuel filter is 34 microns\u2014a homogenizer is required between the purifier and the filter. The agglomerated asphaltenes will choke the filter, and cause excess back flushing \u2013which increases the oil quantity to be incinerated.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">121) There is no back flushing arrangement on the tube type tank cleaning heater\u2014after acid cleaning<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">122) Dead ship recovery to be included in the sea trials.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">123) The extreme aft great lake roller fairleads on each side cannot be used due to obstruction from aft winch framo hydraulics\u2014this on such a huge poop deck, where free space is in abundance. .<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">124)The forward liferaft will be carried off in green seas. DONE<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">125)The FW gen overboard and the SW cooling line overboard is a single butterfly valve<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">126)Many thin drain lines of the deck mounted heater have no slope for cargo to drain by gravity. .<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">127)High level ( 95% )and overfill alarm sirens on deck are TOO LOUD, since they are air operated. It is meant to be heard on the ship\u2014not 5 miles away. It causes concentration deadbands and crucial jobs have to be suspended for people to rush inside CCR and cancel the alarm. As you know tanks are usually loaded to 98%--the terminals will compain\u2014there is something called noise pollution\u2014in California ships are fined for such noise pollution , due to residents within miles around complaining. \u2013and in any case we do not want to wake up sleeping watch keepers who keep 6 on 6 off ---this is not conducive to safety.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">128)The superstripping pipelines have to be fitted with a blank upstream of the stack stripping valve at the pump delivery valve. This will prevent cargo from reaching outside the manifold valve ( which is an ABSOLUTE NO NO!!! ) when stripping the stack .<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">129)The framo power pack room in ER, none of the flanges of HP hyd piplines have antisplash tape. NONSENSE.&nbsp; Physical energy is wasted unnecessarily.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">132)There are no relief valves on inlet line of deck heater.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">133)Flame paths of explosion proof lights should not be painted over.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">134)Yard should equip the ship for passing a PSC examination. Valves must be timed all over again.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">141) Every vent on deck must have a name plate and an arrow showing direction of airflow.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">142)The tank cleaning pumps ( 2 nos ) are booster pumps. If sea water ingress into cargo, causing rejection of entire tank content has to be prevented\u2014check nuts have to be put .<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">241)Most water ballast tanks rubber packings ( they are supposed to be something else on a chemical tanker ) have been glued on with poor adhesive and are coming loose. This is criminal. The insulation is not Chemical vapor proof \u2013say toluene . Even epoxy paint on the insulation will crack it . Conduit branches are not properly caulked to prevent salt water ingress.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">246)The stbd slop UTI tube is bent\u2014due to lack of space..<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">247)To connect the Framo hyd flexible for portable framo test\u2014the fire line had to be loosened and pulled with chain block.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">248)Whose idea is it to fit&nbsp; 3 large capacity AE \u2013which do NOT have enough consumers\u2014<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">--No Bow thruster, <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">--2 Diesel Engines for Framo power pack<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">Low load operation problems using 380 cst HO, with subsequent smoking stacks and carbonization problems , have to be addressed.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">249)There is no stand to do maintenance on the Emg fire pump\u2014top panel. line-height: 150%;\">255) The high emg fire pump suction will take in cavitation air bubbles from the propeller wash\u2014 it is too close and above the propeller. The 150 mm suction pipe has a resistance factor of 4 nos&nbsp; 90 deg bends. The sea water has to rise 7 metres to reach the pump casing\u2014and that too without a foot valve.&nbsp; If you calculate the pressure drop , it is just too much for a vacuum pump to fill up the pump casing with sea water of SG 1.025. The USCG will arrest the ship if the pump does not deliver within 2 minutes of starting the motor. The mech seal will overheat in 2 min. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">256)Though grit blasting has not taken place on the ship for weeks\u2014there is too much grit and plastic garbage all over the ship. Grit in cargo tanks will scour the Framo pump cargo seals and cause wear ring leak. Grit will entrapped by grease and will form grinding paste. Plastic inside ballast tanks with submerged ballast pumps is undesired. The ship must be cleaned up.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">257)The numerous Framo diesel engine flexibles are all held by a single jubilee clip.&nbsp; <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">258)UTI tubes constitute a restricted type of gauging and are not suitable for toxic cargoes. margin-left: 0.5in;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">534)Radar mast looks like an oil rig platform\u2014there is bound to be excessive false echoes.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-left: 0.5in;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">535)Portable framo hyd pipe appears to have cross threaded damage as oil seeps.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-left: 0.5in;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">536)O rings used in ER for fuel filters appear to be poor quality.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-left: 0.5in;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">537)Stuffing box drain tank suction pipe has a hole 10 cms from top and 1 metre from bottom\u2014it should have been reverse.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-left: 0.5in;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">538)Some motors have plastic impellers fans\u2014when motors are run on high loads these toys will melt.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoListParagraph\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-left: 69.75pt; mso-list: l9 level2 lfo12; text-indent: -33.75pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">539)24</span><span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">os toilet skids have poor quality hot water flexible tubes\u2014already 2 have burst.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-left: 0.5in;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">540)ODMCS remote overboard valve is connected to underwater annex 2 line .<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-left: 0.5in;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">541)Reefer alarm hooter does not work.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-left: 0.5in;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">542)Bridge wing life buoy pin has no stopper which will prevent it from falling off due to gravity and vibrations.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-left: 0.5in;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">543)There is no proper ventilation for the purifier room\u2014LEL shows a constant 5%. PCBs\u2019 and electronics are bound to get damaged. The sensor heat setting is only 54 deg c\u2014it should be ambient plus 30 deg C.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-left: 0.5in;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">544)Most FW and fuel tanks have a difference between actual and remote soundings / volumes. Pressure transmitter outputs to be re-adjusted.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-left: 0.5in;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">545)All bollards on deck are undersized\u2014the friction factor afforded to modern hawsers are very less\u2014the ropes are bound to surge and kill somebody.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-left: 0.5in;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">546)PLC interfacings between 2 different manufacturers with different protocols are poor.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-left: 0.5in;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">547)UMS alarms in the day rooms of engineers are not loud enough to wake a sleeper in the bedroom.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-left: 0.5in;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">548)All FRESH water cooling is done in the ER with hard water, without treatment\u2014heat exchange is very less due to scale build up.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-left: 0.5in;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">549)It is apparent that port side spools will not fit on the stbd side\u2014the way the manifold is configured.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-left: 0.5in;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">550)There is no blank on the PV breaker\u2014so minus 60 deg C dew point of nitrogen delivery is just a wild dream.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-left: 40.5pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">551)Most ballast pumping has to be sucked uphill using a huge dia GRE pipe\u2014loading of cargo will have to wait for SBT deballasting when ship has to load to loadlines.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-left: 40.5pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">552)There is high consumption of boiler feed water. Steam traps have not been configured well in the ER.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-left: 40.5pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">553)Cannot start Framo power pumps if the DMP is less than 100 mm AQ\u2014this ship is a chemical tanker where tankdomes have to be kept open while squeezing veg oils or stripping steam condensate. If this is not done up ship staff will be forced to use jumper technology.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-left: 40.5pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">554)Tankcleaning hydrant are also COW line hydrants\u2014they must have a blanking arrangement\u2014not just a dust cap.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-left: 40.5pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">555)No magnetic compass correction Cplath wooden box with spares can be seen anywhere. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-left: 40.5pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">556)There are only 2 pairs scuppers on main deck\u2014one right forward and the other right aft. No scupper has been provided amidship.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-left: 40.5pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">557)Radar mast is like an oil rig\u2014 with low mounted scanners \u2013 see the picture ---there will be too many false echoes\u2014dangerous for navigation. &nbsp;When entering a crowded anchorage radar use is impossible.&nbsp; I expect a collision within the first year after delivery at a crowded anchorage in poor visibility. (<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow;\"> proved true later , by a 2<sup>nd</sup> command master</span>).</span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; line-height: 150%;\">558)There is no drain cock aft of VRL.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-left: 40.5pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">559)The pipeline configurations on deck show that \u2013many cracks can be expected as teething problems.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoListParagraph\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-left: 40.5pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">560)Our refrigerant Compressor running on 134a, has been filled with mineral oil Castrol 299. Excessive 134 a dissolves in mineral oil, which will cause foaming in crankcase, destroying the lubricant properries.&nbsp; crankcase pressure dropping suddenly on compressor startip causes the refrigerant to boil out of oil--THIS IS WHAT FOAMING IS ALL ABOUT to the layman. Usually oil separated out in the evaporator and NOT condenser. Refrigerant 134a REQUIRES \"ESTER BASED\" COMPRESSOR OIL --NOTHING ELSE CAN HANDLE IT!!!--PERIOD!!<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoListParagraph\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-left: 40.5pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">561)Apparently the non return valve of the fresh water generator , is fitted wrong . A guarantee FWG technician to sail with ship from delivery port to next port.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoListParagraph\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-left: 40.5pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">562)After installing PLC and microprocessors in ECR, rampant welding has been done without channeling the return currents using a return current cable. All PLC programming are bound to be corrupted. I expect a delay after dropping the pilot, till the main engine PLC are reprogrammed by Llyngso technician. Be forewarned.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoListParagraph\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-left: 40.5pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">563)Since the cargo tank PV vents are inserted into a hole on main deck on top of tank, with NO reverse U tube rise, I expect cargo to go into engine room and destroy the nitrogen plant membranes. What a disgrace!<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-left: 40.5pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-left: 40.5pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">564) ODMCS overvoard remote Annex 1 valve is connected to Annex 2 overboard.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-left: 40.5pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-left: 40.5pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">565) All mooring bollards are undersize, for the dia of the ship\u2019s hawsers.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-left: 40.5pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-left: 40.5pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">566) Spools from Stbd size manifold cannot be used on port side , as the templating is haywire.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-left: 40.5pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-left: 40.5pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">567) There is NO blanking arrangement for PV breaker ( this is a chemical tanker )<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-left: 40.5pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-left: 40.5pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">568)The ship will take too long to deballast SBT.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-left: 40.5pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">569) All exterior accdn floodlights have por cable sealings. There is bound to be low insulation alarms.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-left: 40.5pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-left: 40.5pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">570) Navtex does NOT have a printer.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-left: 40.5pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-left: 40.5pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">571) It is not possible to start cargo tank framo pumps if the tank pressure is less than 100 mm Aq. This is unfeasible as crew have to dry the sumps after tankcleaning, with tanks under atmospheric pressure ( or while squeegeeing veg oils )<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: center;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-I_d8U_Gohqo/TlCmgcuf9zI/AAAAAAAAFjY/e5GTkLa-JoA/s1600/untitledxc.png\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"400\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-I_d8U_Gohqo/TlCmgcuf9zI/AAAAAAAAFjY/e5GTkLa-JoA/s1600/untitledxc.png\" width=\"295\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nIn July 1997, I was on leave.<br />\n<br />\nIt was raining cats and dogs, which is nothing new in our neck of the woods. During the  SE monsoons  in Kerala , it pours -- it does NOT rain.<br />\n<br />\nAt around 1500 hrs I told my wife that I will be keeping our car at my friends house, on a hill. I said \"I expect the car porch to be flooded and water will enter the car\". <br />\n<br />\nAs I was driving away, all my friends in the neighborhood were having a bullshit session. They waved out to me to join them for a moment.<br />\n<br />\nAll wanted to know where I was going off in a hurry. &nbsp; I said \" I expect all the houses in our neighborhood to have water inside in another 16 hours\".<br />\n<br />\nThey all had a nice laugh, as our area had never been flooded in recent memory, &nbsp;of at least 150 years. And in any case, &nbsp;our city was at the seashore. <br />\n<br />\nAfter I came back, I got all valuable furniture in the ground floor raised , by putting bricks. This also included the fridges, washing machine, electric oven etc. I bought a bottle of kerosene and kept it standby.<br />\n<br />\nWe went to sleep at around 10 PM.<br />\n<br />\nWe were woken up in the morning at around 5 am, by a call from my neighbor, that water had entered their house. So I came down with my wife and found we had another 11 inches to go before water entered our home. Within another 50 minutes I saw 11 inches being covered up, and water started pouring inside the house.<br />\n<br />\nI poured some Kerosene in all the flooding rooms. The water stopped rising and remained steady when it was about 10 inches above the floor. I had predicted the stop in rising water too.<br />\n<br />\nAt sunrise there was a huge collective effort to push all the cars in the neighborhood to the highest place . Water had entered into all the cars, and none of them could be started.<br />\n<br />\nThen I got a call from another neighbor that a small snake had been found in one of their bedrooms, and there was general panic. I said, in my house kerosene has taken care of it. And then all were tripping over each other to do Kerosene honours. Snakes dread Kerosene, as it destroys their skin and burns it, causing severe pain.<br />\n<br />\nSo pretty soon, &nbsp;the talk in the neighbour hood was \" Ajit is the only smart fuc#er amongst us, as usual \u2014he did NOT lose a dang thing!\".<br />\n<br />\nSome of their houses had ruined their super expensive drawing room sofas , costing them a huge financial package.<br />\n<br />\nMy wife told me \u201c So far so good-- how did your know, that the water will enter our houses? \u201c<br />\n<br />\nI said : \u201cBlame it on El Nino!\u201d<br />\n<br />\nShe looked at me as if I had gone crazy. <br />\n<br />\nThen she asked \" How did you know the water will stop rising ?\u201d.<br />\n<br />\nI said \u201c It is obvious that the nearest dam operators , have clandestinely opened the locks , to release excess water, above the red danger mark, the dam is NOT constructed for, or capable of handling. Of course they will never ever admit it. Water from heavy rains cannot raise ground water so fast, when we are at the sea coast .\u201d<br />\n<br />\nAfter a month I joined a ship at Coos bay Oregon, ( West coast USA ) in the end of Aug 1997. This ship was a nice multipurpose bulk carrier. There was an emergency as the Nickel concentrate from New Caledonia loaded in heavy rain ,  had liquefied, and company wanted  me to handle the discharge, though I was NOT a bulk carrier man.<br />\n<br />\nWhile at the hotel before joining , I read in the newspapers about local fishermen complaining that they cant catch a single fish in usual fish rich waters. Well the fish had swum up to colder waters to survive.  <br />\n<br />\nAfter sailing off from Coos bay to Manzanillo, Mexico to load cement in Bulk. Enroute, I saw several dead whales floating on water. Obviously they died due to the heated water.<br />\n<br />\nOn the way, I planned my passage to be away from a Hurricane area on the West coast of Mexico. The Charterers and Passage planning whizkids frowned. &nbsp;But I was right, there was indeed a vicious hurricane which formed suddenly, almost out of thin air \u2014and we were lucky to be seawards and safe. As the mid ship hold could NOT be flooded with heavy weather ballast. <br />\n<br />\nThen we proceeded to Chile to discharge the cement, at a small port on the seaside of the Andes. The Atacama desert, the driest on the planet, where NO life sustains, &nbsp;lay on the other side.<br />\n<br />\nAs we berthed , I told my Chief officer still at forward stations. \u201c There will be NO cargo work today, after the hold cargo surface inspections , and draft survey is done , I want you to shut all the hatchcovers\u201d<br />\n<br />\nThe pilot intervened \u201c Why Captain, are you afraid , it will rain? . Rest your fears , it has NOT rained in this port Antofagasta for the past 100 years. My wife got sick and tired of daily rain at Valpraiso ( Asthma ) , South of this port, and this is why we got ourselves transferred here.\u201d<br />\n<br />\nI said \u201c It will rain tonight!\u201d <br />\n<br />\nThe pilot looked at me as if I was an unreasonable tyrant cum nut-case &nbsp;, shrugged his shoulders and left.<br />\n<br />\nThe next day, morning at 0700 hrs I get a knock on my door and there stood the pilot, with a beaming face. \u201c Captain, it rained yesterday night for one hour \u201c <br />\n<br />\nI said \u201c I know, for while coming back from the strip tease bar, with my Chief officer, we got drenched in rain\u201d.<br />\n<br />\nAnd then the pilot would NOT leave till I told him my secret.<br />\n<br />\nSo I told him \u201c Well, pilot , 1997 is the El Nino year!\u201d<br />\n<br />\nAfter discharge at Antofagasta, we sailed to Equador ( Esmeraldes ) to load logs. This ship could be converted to a Timber carrier or a Container ship.  <br />\n<br />\nThere is a river which flows across the mouth of the entrance to this port. The pilot came on board with his trainee, and just at the entrance , sensing impending disaster, I wrested control of the ship from him, and did the berthing myself.<br />\n<br />\nThe pilot was terribly upset, that I did this in front of his trainee, and naturally he confronted me, telling me that this is the first time in 23 years someone has belittled him in this fashion. <br />\n<br />\nI said \u201c You have positioned the tug at the wrong place, you have NO idea how the strong current of the river in todays flood torrent, which will jack knife the ship using the wind.\u201d<br />\n<br />\nSure enough, as soon as we berthed, even the Agent, Customs, Immigration, Port health etc knew that I was a racist Master who did NOT trust the local pilot. &nbsp;I could sense the hostility.<br />\n<br />\nThe agent told me \u201c Captain, tomorrow the Harbour Master wants to have a word with you. Be careful Captain, these pilots are all very proud of their expertise and you have just rubbed their faces into the ground. Better keep a good explanation ready. It is a small port, &nbsp;and we all know each other \u201d.<br />\n<br />\nThe next day at around 0800 hrs, I was on the bridge wing. I could see another ship approaching to take the berth ahead of us. The Pilot lost control at the entrance and put the engines full throttle, the tug pushed the wrong way, the way it always did, and sure enough, the ship was coming to hit us at right angles.<br />\n<br />\nI raced down to my cabin , got the camera , and started taking shots, in succession. The last 30 metres of the approach, how the ships bows crumpled at our hull near No 2 hold, severely damaging 3 timber staunchions and the entire bulwark, all was captured in the camera, with time shots of the GPS in between-- a no contest situation. <br />\n<br />\nWithin one hour the Harbour Master was in my cabin.<br />\n<br />\n&nbsp;He said \u201c Captain, I had interviewed the trainee pilot yesterday, &nbsp;he is related to my wife .  He told me that you had predicted this yesterday!. He had told me about the strong river cross-current , you pointed out at the entrance . The pilots on board the other ship, are the same two. How did you predict all this? \u201d<br />\n<br />\nI said \u201c Well , it is the El Nino year!\u201d.<br />\n<br />\nTo my surprise he knew what the El Nino was.<br />\n<br />\nThen I took a lot of provisions, and told the Charterers and the company that I expect a delay at the Panama canal with our max Panama canal draft. They disagreed with me.<br />\n<br />\nSure enough, we were delayed at Balboa for more than one week. It rains in Panama canal daily, so much that they need shelters at the bridge wings for the Pilot. But now, in 1997 there was no rain at all. <br />\n<br />\nNobody was willing to declare that there is less water in the Gatun lake. Every time, they opened the locks, they lost precious fresh water from the lake. So they were doing the operations in such a way, that they lost minimum water. At Gatun lake I told the pilot I do NOT want to anchor in the usual area.<br />\n<br />\nThe pilot asked me why?  I said there is less water. Immediately the pilot said. \u201c Damn! , Captain,  you are absolutely right. On my last 3 ships, I felt the &nbsp;drag under the ship, with vibrations and muddly wake. All on &nbsp;the bridge including myself, Master and OOW pretended all is OK. <br />\n<br />\nWe all pretended to sleep and expected the other to wake us up. But the angry Engineers demanded by several telephone calls\u2014what the hell is happening on bridge?<br />\n<br />\nThen we went to Spain , Huelva, to discharge , and all there said the weather is totally unseasonal.<br />\n<br />\nSoon we were in Parana river Argentina. The river had flooded 4.5 metres above normal. Even the quay godowns were under water, and we could see just the tip of the roofs. I was told by the greedy shippers, to load to a deeper draft, and I refused.<br />\n<br />\nI was alone against everybody--the bag unreasonable guy. I said, the river might be deep, due to excess rain in the Brazilian rain forest of Matto Grosso. But where the river meets the sea, at Recalada, and else where the depths are still the same. <br />\n<br />\nAfter lot of missiles by telexes up and down, I won. I knew my rights. Nobody can arm twist Vadakayil.<br />\n<br />\nThe ship had to go to Montevideo to top up with logs and then go to Tofte, Norway. At Montevideo, the ship was sitting merrily on the bottom mud.<br />\n<br />\nAfter the deck level came two high ( of unbarked Eucalpytus log bundles ), I gave sufficient notice, that I will load only 3 high\u2014NOT 4 high as originally planned by the British Supercargo Captain, who had been doing this for 18 years--on sister ships.<br />\n<br />\nI gave my reasons, several of them -- including Stability calculations , with virtual loss of GM due to upthrust . And to top it all even NAABSA clause did NOT exist in the charter party.<br />\n<br />\nThe last of the several reasons was the \"snow factor\", on arrival Norway. That the ship with GM of about 40 cms , would be destabilized by the weight of snow on the 4th layer. <br />\n<br />\nThe Norwegian Director of the Charterers ( no names ) send me a sarcastic telex . \u201c Captain, we are already into March 1998 , and so far Norway did NOT have a single minute of snow.<br />\n<br />\nMy daughters are very disappointed over this. The winter is over, Captain--period!.  We require you to load the 4th layer, failing which we will take your company to court!\u201d<br />\n<br />\nMy Tech managers shat green peas, as soon as they read this , and they ordered me to load the 4th layer, \"under protest\".<br />\n<br />\nAll I said was \u201c This is the El Nino year. I will bring snow to Norway, in the end of March 1998 !\u201d<br />\n<br />\nThe day we arrived Norway, a technical team was earmarked to have a Stability Mathematics calculation Olympiad with me. They all came on board, along with the Top Gun of the company.<br />\n<br />\nThis man said \u201c Captain, I was NOT supposed to come. But-- here is the telex, where you declared that you will bring snow to Norway. How right you were!. All or roads are blocked by the most severe blizzard of the decade, and the winter is officially over 1 month ago !\u201d<br />\n<br />\nI broke the seal of the company mail packet, and took our the Company magazine, in which I had written a piece on El Nino and La Nina, and gave it to the Big Boss.<br />\n<br />\nAfter reading it said :  \u201c Can I take this copy with me ?. You and me are the same kind-- we don\u2019t care for past practice. We carry our own lamps and we chart our own way.\u201d.<br />\n<br />\nAfter this statement, &nbsp;the Maths Olympiad party looked pretty deflated, and melted away with their tails between their legs.<br />\n<br />\n<i><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue;\">So here is a gist of what I wrote about El Nino. </span></i><br />\n<br />\nThe El Nino starts after a pool of hot seawater almost the size of USA, ( more than 15 million square kms ) appears off the west coast of the Americas. The ocean would heat up right around Christmas time, so fishermen call the phenomenon El Ni\u00f1o, for the Christ Child.<br />\n<br />\nUsually, the wind blows strongly from east to west along the equator in the Pacific. This actually piles up water (about half a meter's worth) in the western part of the Pacific. In the eastern part, deeper water (which is colder than the sun-warmed surface water) gets pulled up from below to replace the water pushed west. So, the normal situation is warm water (about 30 C) in the west, cold (about 22 C) in the east.<br />\n<br />\nIn an El Ni\u00f1o, the winds pushing that water around get weaker. As a result, some of the warm water piled up in the west slumps back down to the east, and not as much cold water gets pulled up from below. Both these tend to make the water in the eastern Pacific warmer, which is one of the hallmarks of an El Ni\u00f1o.<br />\n<br />\nBut it doesn't stop there. The warmer ocean then affects the winds--it makes the winds weaker! So if the winds get weaker, then the ocean gets warmer, which makes the winds get weaker, which makes the ocean get warmer ... this is called a positive feedback, and is what makes an El Ni\u00f1o grow.<br />\n<br />\nThe ocean has a wave called a Rossby wave that is quite unlike the waves you see when you visit the beach. It's more like a distant cousin to a tidal wave. The difference is that a tidal wave goes very quickly, with all the water moving pretty much in the same direction. In a Rossby wave, the upper part of the ocean, say the top 100 meters or so, will be leisurely sliding one way, while the lower part, starting at 100 meters and going on down, will be slowly moving the other way. <br />\n<br />\nAfter a while they switch directions. Everything happens very slowly and inside the ocean, and you can't even see them on the surface. These things are so slow, they can take months or years to cross the oceans. If you had the patience to sit there while one was going by, you'd hardly notice it; the water would be moving only 1/100th of walking speed. But they are large, hundreds or thousands of kilometers in length (not height! Remember, you can hardly see them on the surface), so they can have an effect on things. <br />\n<br />\nAnother wave you rarely hear about is called a Kelvin wave, and it has some characteristics in common with Rossby waves, but is somewhat faster and can only exist close to the equator (say, within about 5 degrees of latitude around the equator). El Ninos often start with a Kelvin wave propagating from the western Pacific over towards South America. <br />\n<br />\nWhen an El Ni\u00f1o gets going in the middle or eastern part of the Pacific, it creates Rossby waves that drift slowly towards southeast Asia. After several months of travelling, they finally get near the coast and reflect back. The changes in interior ocean temperature that these waves carry with it \"cancel out\" the original temperature changes that made the El Ni\u00f1o in the first place. A strong El Ni\u00f1o can last a year or more before conditions return to normal.  <br />\n<br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: red; font-size: large;\">The 1997/1998, is the strongest El Ni\u00f1o in recorded history, and it had more energy than a hundred Hiroshima bombs</span><br />\n<br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; color: blue; font-size: large;\"><b>El Nino causes droughts and forest fires in Australia and also bleaching of corals ( loss of CO2 due to warming of waters ).&nbsp;</b></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue;\"><br /></span>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue;\">The hurricanes in the East of USA reduces , by the typhoons in the Pacific become more and stronger.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<br />\nIn 1997 , the surface temperatures of the Pacific Ocean off the coasts of Ecuador and Peru rose to about 5 C above normal. Instrumentation Buoys in the Pacific Ocean.<br />\n<br />\n&nbsp;The giant El Ni\u00f1o of 1997-98 had deranged weather patterns around the world, killed an estimated 2,200 people, and caused more than 35 billion USD dollars in property damage.<br />\n<br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue; font-size: large;\">2010 was the year of the La Nina\u2014the strongest in recorded history</span>.<br />\n<br />\nThe Nina is the Yang of the Nino Yin.&nbsp; <br />\n<br />\nAustralia had horrific floods. The name La Ni\u00f1a originates from Spanish, meaning \"the girl\", analogous to El Ni\u00f1o meaning \"the boy\"..<br />\n<br />\nLa Ni\u00f1a is often preceded by a strong El Ni\u00f1o.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; Ajit Vadakayil", "url": "https://www.blogger.com/profile/14410812789424637654", "image": {"url": "//4.bp.blogspot.com/-QSnd-Z8F7Kc/XFtPudWdwlI/AAAAAAABfq4/vxrkFOO7Iu8Mf6-OaPgw6FPpRDSmMgLdgCK4BGAYYCw/s35/capt%25252BajitC%25252Bvadakayil.JPG"}}, "replies": {"totalItems": "38", "selfLink": "https://www.googleapis.com/blogger/v3/blogs/3564735312144269387/posts/7714949272693422936/comments"}}, {"kind": "blogger#post", "id": "5258879302368700069", "blog": {"id": "3564735312144269387"}, "published": "2011-02-17T10:32:00+05:30", "updated": "2019-03-04T20:31:53+05:30", "etag": "\"iHf3yWDE_geBgZ8U7rgZ_xuTeAQ/dGltZXN0YW1wOiAxNTUxNzExNzEzODA4Cm9mZnNldDogMTk4MDAwMDAK\"", "url": "http://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.com/2011/02/diabolical-ministering-angel-mother.html", "selfLink": "https://www.googleapis.com/blogger/v3/blogs/3564735312144269387/posts/5258879302368700069", "title": "DIABOLICAL MINISTERING ANGEL MOTHER TERESA -- CAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL", "content": "<div dir=\"ltr\" style=\"text-align: left;\" trbidi=\"on\">\n<div dir=\"ltr\" style=\"text-align: left;\" trbidi=\"on\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 24px;\">MOTHER TERESA THE MOST OVER RATED PERSON IN HISTORY--&nbsp; THE EVIL SAINT WHO CONVERTED&nbsp; HUMAN BEINGS&nbsp; MINUTES BEFORE DYING -- MUNCHAUSEN SYNDROME BY PROXY</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-mFpq5dqmNS0/TVyp9wfalRI/AAAAAAAADdg/QhYlZLpCysM/s1600/download.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"320\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-mFpq5dqmNS0/TVyp9wfalRI/AAAAAAAADdg/QhYlZLpCysM/s320/download.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 16px;\">&nbsp;&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">I am aware that this post will not endear me to a lot of my regular readers. But then what has to be said must be said, truth cannot be subverted . I do not wish to win popularity contests. I am the master of my will and slave of my conscience. Still i will feel bad while typing all what follows.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 16px;\">&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">One day myself and my wife saw an old lady lying on the streets , totally blind ,emaciated and helpless.&nbsp; I slowed down the car. Suddenly I recognised this lady . When I was a&nbsp; young child , she had worked in my house as a part time cook for a while. I roughly calculated here age to be 90.&nbsp;&nbsp; She could not recognize me, was out of her mind and incoherent due to her sufferings. There was no way i could leave her there, in that state.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">So we carried her , placed her in our car, and drove home. I then rang up Mother Theresa\u2019s home at Calicut for destitutes, and explained the situation . The curt answer was, that they do NOT collect destitutes . They take in only the ones brought in by the police or the Calicut corporation. Now, I have donated a lot of my own hard earned money to Mother Theresa and party, and that made me very resolute.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">So we cleaned up this old destitute and took her in our car to the Mother Theresa home at Calicut. After waiting in the office for an eternal 10 minutes, the head nun sauntered in .. To cut a long story short, she refused to take the old lady . Her&nbsp; argument was that they are full up.&nbsp; <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Then another amazing&nbsp; argument \u201d This lady was your ex-cook, it is your duty to care of her till she dies !\u201d&nbsp; Totally pissed off , I told her off \u201c Don\u2019t give me unwanted advise . I have donated XXX thousand rupees to the Theresa charity foundation over several years , and I would be taking up the matter, with your HO in Calcutta.&nbsp; Immediately she became eager-beaver , her tone changed and she was ready to take the old lady in.&nbsp; My wife said \u201c No, let us take her to the Muncipality city home for destitutes\u201d&nbsp; and that is where she died after a year. (I pulled strings with my next door neighbour-- the Mayor of Calicut-- and got her in.)<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">I have never ever donated after this incident to Charity foundations. This incident killed something inside me.</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">My wife still does here charity work secretly ( it is all my money, quite a percentage&nbsp; ) . I get to know about this from grateful letters, cash receipts etc she has hidden under table cloths or dark corners, and I say nothing nor ask her why? Most of her donations are to hospitals and orphanages for free meals to the poor. Religion, caste and creed is no bar. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">True philanthropists will never ever seek publicity. Right?<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">What I write below has been gleaned from many insiders and also from my own experiences . The majority of Mother Theresa\u2019s nuns were from my home state of Kerala, as there is a tradition to give a daughter in sacrifice as a nun, for financial favours received from the powerful and rich Church. And usually the ugliest girl child would be earmarked. You can hardly find a beautiful nun among the Kerala nuns. They all know deep inside that they are ugly duckling discards.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">As a young 2nd officer, my ship was at Livorno , with no cargo work for 2 days , due to Easter .&nbsp; Myself, the Captain , 2nd Engr and Purser went to Rome. The Purser was a Roman Catholic from Goa was with us and he had made contact with his cousin brother who was a monk in a monastery , Casa Palotti at Vatican.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">So we went there first, a large building by the side of the river Tiber, full of Roman Catholic nuns and brothers. We got free accommodation in their guest quarters. We saw Rome , listened to the Pope\u2019s speech from the Vatican palace balcony, watched the smoke wisps, and came back at night dog tired .&nbsp; Just after dinner at the common mess, 3 Malayalam speaking nuns ( my lingo party from kerala&nbsp; ) came to see me and talk for a while.&nbsp; <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Being young and naive I gasped \u201c Wow! you are the prettiest looking Kerala nuns I have ever seen!\u201d.
