She would force Indian Airlines to fly here nuns free. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">It was all about the holy Spirit guiding the holy Mother.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">In her Nobel acceptance speech , she went on and on on , how she roamed the dark, damp and dangerous Calcutta streets to pick up the destitute. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">BULLSHIT !. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">She gave away the ambulances , she received as donations. She did NOT pick anybody nor did she allow her clan to pick up. Only destitutes brought in by the Calcutta Corporation was considered.&nbsp; Some of her ambulances were used only to transport her nuns to Churches for prayer and to Airports and Train stations.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Blah Blah-- \"We have a home for the dying in Calcutta, where we have picked up more than 36000 people only from the streets of Calcutta, and out of that big number more than 18000 have died a beautiful death. They have just gone home to God.\"&nbsp; WOW!<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Sometimes while giving her speech, she would say, that she fed 10000 people . Then after 3 minutes this figure would come down to 4000, and then jump back to 9000\u2014 yet nobody was sarcastic of her true lies.. While actually she would just be feeding 300, and only those who has a food coupon, mostly converted and baptised Christians.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">She would say \u201d If there was poor leper on the moon, I will be the first to be there!\u201d, and all cried WOW, -- egged on by the Vatican sponsored press.&nbsp; <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">She was grateful to the Vatican , for their fantastic propaganda , and hence in return campaigned relentlessly against abortion. Her entire obsession was that the raped women if pregnant must not have abortions. She would never fly abroad, unless she stopped over at the Pope\u2019s residence. <o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-XmnEszQu4Z0/TVyrZMTP-dI/AAAAAAAADdw/nSAAhyO-EYM/s1600/images+%25284%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"320\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-XmnEszQu4Z0/TVyrZMTP-dI/AAAAAAAADdw/nSAAhyO-EYM/s320/images+%25284%2529.jpg\" width=\"280\" /></a></div>\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">A very poor and very ill child would not be offered help unless the parents signed (or thumb-printed) a form of renunciation signing over the rights of the child to her organisation.&nbsp; There is video evidence of such a case happening on the doorstep of Mother Teresa's orphanage.&nbsp; <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">In her Nobel Prize speech Mother Teresa had said that in 6 years in Calcutta there were \"61,273 babies less\" born because of her organisation's natural family planning activities. There is no basis whatever for this accurate statistics, it surprised even her well wishers--&nbsp; it was diabolical&nbsp; of Mother Teresa to mention it in her Nobel Prize speech.<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-yFk0Sp_KDyg/TVyrdJ_ShVI/AAAAAAAADd0/aQcHh5rlfaY/s1600/images+%25281%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"292\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-yFk0Sp_KDyg/TVyrdJ_ShVI/AAAAAAAADd0/aQcHh5rlfaY/s320/images+%25281%2529.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">In the April 1996 issue of the US magazine Ladies Home Journal, Mother Teresa said that she wanted to die like the poor in her home for the dying destitute in Kalighat. This is a white lie as she always went abroad for medical treatments . She also had several treatments at expensive Calcutta's Woodlands and Belle Vue Clinics, which are outside the reach of 99% of India's population. Her Calcutta nuns just had to suffer out a tooth ache and take a bath in just one bucket of cold water, though she was worth billions. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Virgin sister Susan Shields who handled incoming money in NY USA remembers that one year itself, she personally handled donations of more than $50 million in a New York bank account. She had testified that all money came , clearly marked \" for the destitute \", from world wide, and was NOT for opening fresh Catholic institutions.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Computers, typewriters, photocopiers are not allowed. Even when they are donated, they are not allowed to be installed. For book-keeping the sisters use school notebooks, in which they write in cramped pencilled figures. Until they are full. Then everything is erased and the cheap notebook is used again. All ostensibly in order to save. It was basically to fool others into believing she was poor. The real reason was to cover up her tracks and avoid getting audited ..<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-LQAWHOHxWjs/UTGCN5ZstFI/AAAAAAAAgRk/_npImOqR5DQ/s1600/dfwgd.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"192\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-LQAWHOHxWjs/UTGCN5ZstFI/AAAAAAAAgRk/_npImOqR5DQ/s320/dfwgd.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 16px;\">In 1984 Mother Teresa (publicly) declined the offer of cataract surgery from the St Francis Medical Centre in Pittsburgh, USA, telling the media that she could not possibly accept the \u00a35000 treatment, and the Vatican made everybody say WOW!&nbsp; In secret she had the same surgery (which cost even more) in St Vincent's Hospital , New York.</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The destitutes in her Calcutta home was not given the smallest iota of dignity and care or even pain killers.&nbsp; It was all a big sham. It was about suffering for Jesus, the same way he had suffered for us. The nuns did whatever they could in all humility, in the hope that Jesus will reward them. These poor nuns were even forced to vote for the political party she chose.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">It was compulsory for women to shave their heads, just because Mother Theresa was bald.&nbsp; She knew very well of the particular cultural importance Indian women (however poor or destitute) attach to long hair.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 16px;\">&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Occasionally when on board the first class section of an aeroplane, Mother Teresa would demand for left over food to be given her so that she could take them to the poor. This would impress all the rich folks around her and all would say WOW and \u201c way to go! \u201c and clap.&nbsp; The moment she got of the plane she would dump the unwieldy food into the nearest dustbin. It was all about positive word of mouth publicity. The saint would keep repeating that she never did anything that would detract from the cause of the poor.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">She was an exceptional Catholic -- indeed much (if not most) of the resources of her organisation was spent on religious activities, such as in the training of nuns, novices, Brothers and priests, and in the upkeep of establishments which are exclusively nunneries and Brothers' houses. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">When Mother Teresa told journalists (as she did very often during her life) how many establishments she ran around the world, she never made it clear that a large number of these housed Catholic nuns and brothers and were not homes for the poor, for which cause money poured in .<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">In December 1984, 25000 people died in Bhopal from inhaling MDI cyanide toxic gas, leaked by the multinational giant Union Carbide, the Vatican send her to broker for Catholic Chairman Warren Anderson. Warren Anderson made a huge pay off of Union Carbide money .&nbsp; Mother Teresa, whose post-Nobel reputation within India was then very high indeed, rushed in to Bhopal like an international dignitary. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 16px;\">&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">She looked at the carnage, nodded gravely three times and said, \"I say, forgive.\" There was a stunned silence in the audience and press. She took in the incredulity, nodded again, glared back and repeated, \"I say, forgive\". Then she quickly wafted away, like visiting royalty.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Mother Teresa's propaganda machinery handled her Bhopal trip in the following clever but diabolical way:<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">QUOTE-- As she was present to the agony of Calcutta, and that of India's other great cities, so Mother Teresa was present to the anguish of Bhopal, a city four hundred miles to the south of Delhi, when a cloud of smoke enveloped a crowded slum on the night of December 3, 1984. The Missionaries of Charity, who had long been working in Bhopal, escaped being among the victims because the death-bringing gas was blown by the wind in a different direction....... Even while the dead were being cremated or buried, Mother Teresa rushed to Bhopal with teams of Missionaries of Charity to work with the Sisters already on the scene. \"We have come to love and care for those who most need it in this terrible tragedy\", said Mother Teresa, as she went from centre to centre, from hospital to hospital visiting afflicted people-- .UNQUOTE<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Another of Mother's biographies has a photograph in it with the following caption: \"Helping A Survivor of the Chemical Leak at Bhopal, December 1984\".The photograph concerned shows Mother daintily offering a marigold flower to a woman moribundly lying in a hospital bed.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">After 26 years , dead souls got a pittance of 500 USD as compensation -- This is American \"Agent Orange Justice\" for you.&nbsp; ( The Indian IPL cricket league is worth&nbsp; 4 billion USD )<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br />\nShe did the same for Charles Keating--who gave her a huge bribe. <span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\">Teresa had admitted that&nbsp;she received at least $1,250,000 - but it is known that he stole (at least) $253 million, which were the moneys of small investors. Keating also gave Mother the free use of his personal jet and in return he received her blessings and a personalised crucifix, which he carries everywhere. </span><br />\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\"><br />\nIn January 1992, when Keating's fraud trial was still going on in a Los Angeles court, he got more back from his special friend. She wrote a letter to the trial judge Lance Ito (who later became a household name for sitting at the O.J. Simpson trial):<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.5in; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto;\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\"><em>Dear Honorable Lance Ito,</em></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.5in; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto;\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\"><em><br /></em></span>\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\"><em>We do not mix up in Business or Politics or courts...I do not know anything about Mr Charles Keating's work or his business or the matters you are dealing with. ... </em></span></div>\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\"><em>\n</em></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.5in; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto;\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\"><em><br /></em></span>\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\"><em>I only know that he has always been kind and generous to God's poor, and always ready to help whenever there was a need. Whenever someone asks me to speak to a trial judge, I always tell them the same thing. </em></span></div>\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\"><em>\n</em></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.5in; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto;\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\"><em><br /></em></span></div>\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\"><em>\n</em></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.5in; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto;\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\"><em>I ask them to pray, to look into their heart, and to do what Jesus would do in that circumstance. And that is what is I am asking of you, your Honor.</em></span></div>\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\"><em>\n</em></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.5in; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto;\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\"><em><br /></em></span>\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\"><em>My gratitude to you is my prayer for you, and your work, your family and the people you are dealing with. </em></span></div>\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\"><em>\n</em></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.5in; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto;\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\"><em>God Bless You </em></span></div>\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\"><em>\n</em></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.5in; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto;\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\"><em><br /></em></span>\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\"><em>M. Teresa, M.C.</em></span></div>\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\"><em>\n</em></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.5in; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto;\">\n</div>\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\">\n</span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.5in; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto;\">\n<span style=\"color: navy; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\">After Keating's conviction and imprisonment,&nbsp; a pissed off Paul W. Turley, the then Deputy District Attorney of Los Angeles County wrote the following letter to Mother Teresa, hoping to retrive some swindled money: </span><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt 0.5in;\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\"><em>Dear Mother Teresa <o:p></o:p></em></span></div>\n<em>  </em><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.5in; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto;\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\"><em>...The victims of Mr Keating's fraud come from a wide spectrum of society. Some were wealthy and well educated. Most were people of modest means and unfamiliar with high finance. One was, indeed a poor carpenter who did not speak English and had his life's savings stolen by Mr Keating's fraud.</em></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.5in; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto;\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\"><em><br /></em></span>\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\"><em>The Biblical slogan of your organisation is 'As long as you did it to one of My least brethren. You did it to Me.' The 'least' of the brethren are among those whom Mr Keating fleeced without flinching... It is not uncommon for 'con' men to be generous with family, friends and charities...No church, no charity, no organisation should allow itself to be used as salve for the conscience of the criminal. </em></span></div>\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\"><em>\n</em></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.5in; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto;\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\"><em><br /></em></span>\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\"><em>You urge Judge Ito to look into his heart - as he sentences Charles Keating - and do what Jesus would do. I submit the same challenge to you. As she arrived at Rome airport, she was ceremoniously quarantined there. Pictures of her being taken away for quarantine were circulated all over the world by the Pope propaganda machine&nbsp; -- the natural assumption was that she had been working knee deep with plague sufferers. She had had no involvement whatsoever either during or after the plague with treatment or prevention.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Mother Teresa frequently stated that the \"happiest day of my life is when the Holy Father came to Calcutta.\"&nbsp; It is noteworthy that Mother's happiest day was not when she got the divine revelation, or any other day.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">On 18 November, Mother Teresa participated in a dharna (sit-in) and fast in Delhi demanding reservations for dalit low caste Christians. Then suddenly criticism of her actions started flooding in, especially from the Indian media, who are normally sympathetic to her (a lot of resentment exists in India over religion and caste reservations). Even her dear old Calcutta Statesman, published a sarcastic cartoon, Mother Teresa, who moved quite expertly in response to public and media opinion in India, now did an utter volte-face. She took the unprecedented step of calling a press conference (on 24 November) at Mother House in Calcutta and denied all knowledge of the sit-in! She said she thought it was merely a prayer session. Her denial was emphatic: \"I have never participated in any sit-in demonstrations or demanded reservations for dalit Christians.\" A professional politician could not have lied better, despite being on video camera.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 16px;\">&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">One year after her first death anniversary, the German magazine Stern, published a searing critique of her work in an article titled, \"Mother Teresa, Where Are Your Millions?\" An article that took a year's research in three continents and concluded that her organisation did not deserve to be called a charitable foundation, nor she a saint.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 16px;\">&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">On October 18, 2003, India gave up her most famous mother to the world. , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Sorry, this intelligent force which resides in your DNA and preserves the blueprint, is NOT stupid.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">At home when you go for a crap, the fecal matter enters a septic tank. There is NIL oxygen in this tank, only methane. The bacteria inside is called anaerobic bacteria, which processes the shit. This bacteria will die if you open the slab of the pit, and allow oxygen to enter.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">On the ship we have a Sewage treatment plant. Our fecal matter enters this plant, which has a turbo fan running all the time, 24 hrs a day, 365 days a month. The bacteria in this plant is called aerobic bacteria,, as they are oxygen dependant. You put off the fan, and the aerobic bacteria dies. And then the plant stinks.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">The intelligent force called God had meant it this way. This is called the Cosmic dance of Shiva. In Vedas we refer to this as Tamas Rajas. Chinese call it Yin Yang.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">When the Aerobic bacteria dies due to oxygen getting cut off, the Anaerobic bacteria which does NOT require oxygen starts giving birth-- in a smooth manner.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<i><span style=\"color: black; line-height: 115%;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">It is a perfect tango of dynamic balance where one polar opposite changes into another smoothly and constantly</span></span></i><br />\n<br />\n<div>\n<span class=\"apple-style-span\"><i><span style=\"color: black; Many other US firms also jumped into the bandwagon.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">All YE foolish people who drink this packaged stuff-- take this from Capt Vadakayil--&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: red; font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif; font-size: large;\">You must drink the tender coconut water within a minute of exposing the water from the opened coconut to the atmosphere. text-align: justify;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">1) viscous cargo ( possible if the Framo wear rings are worn out )<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">2) due to use of portable framo pump <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">3) excessive back pressure at terminal, and no internal stripping was done.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">The ROB quantity inside tank can be calculated as follows using the wedge formula.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Most surveyors and ships have ready made computer software to do this. The forward part of the aft trimmed tank is empty, and you cannot use the trim tables for ullage volume, that is why you use this formula.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">F= distance of ullage pipe from aft bulkhead (metres).<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">B= breadth of tank (metres)<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">L= LBP of ship (metres)<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">T= trim (metres)<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">S= sounding of liquid (metres)<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">V=volume of liquid (cum)<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">C=corrected sounding (metres)<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">O= trim in degrees <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">D=depth of tank (metres)<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">TanO=T/L<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">C=S+(F - DTanO) TanO ( no UTI tube extension tube )<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">V=L X B X C/ 2T<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Remember\u2014Most of the UTI tubes have a perforated tube extension to the bottom, to prevent the 30 minute moratorium,<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>after completion of loading static cargoes<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>( in absence of inert gas ).&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Wedge formula is applicable for the tape which falls straight through a main deck hole , by gravity-- NOT a tape which lies inside a UTI extension tube at an incline.</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; letter-spacing: 0.05pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;
