Usually i am too busy to see a movie or even go ashore, on my Chemical Tanker.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">I saw this movie, then hit the bed as it was late at night, then got up after 20 minutes of tossing and turning , and saw the movie once more. &nbsp;Next day, I gave the movie DVD back to the Third mate and told him \" I saw this movie twice \".&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">He remarked \" If Capt Vadakayil has seen a movie twice, it means it is worth seeing!\"</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">I said \" I expect this movie to be a total flop all over the world. The producer has put his own plain Jane daughter as the heroine, but she has done a good job. And there is a soul stirring song by some Sufi style Pakistani guy\" .</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Well the singer was the same Pakistani Rahat Khan.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">This brings me back to art. &nbsp;Real art has been buried, by vested interests.<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: red;\">&nbsp;</span></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: red;\"><br />\n</span></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: red;\">So many talented artists and singers have died penniless, yet the pretenders laugh all the way to the bank. It is all about marketing</span>.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Who cares for true talent?</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">A few years ago, i visited an art exhibition at Mumbai--Jehangir art gallery. Among all the paintings displayed, there was NOT A SINGLE painting, which required a vestige of talent. Most of them were abstract modern art. A few realistic landscapes etc, did not have any true perspective or true light sourcing.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">I went to the painter who commanded the highest price, borrowed a sheet of paper and a carbon stick , and drew his face in about 5 minutes - free hand. By some amount of luck it turned out stunningly real. &nbsp;Now, i am the type of guy who performs better, in hostile conditions. I do not care for home crowd advantage. Lot of people gathered around me .&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Then I asked him if he can do the same . His reply was simple \" I don't do human portraits and faces \" . &nbsp;A lady in the crowd sniggered loudly , \" That is because he cannot do it, even if he wanted to. He is THE modern abstract painter\".</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">This reminds me how art has degenerated.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">In school when i was 12 years old, we had a all India CBSE School art contest. My art teacher, called me and told me to make a clay model. I told him that i have never attempted it before. I was a proven good painter , both water color and oil, and had won several trophies for my school at the Calicut district schools level. He suggested that i must make a model of Mother and Child , and dumped a large quantity of clay in my hands.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">I lugged all the clay home, and then i suddenly remembered that one of the local hospitals ( Ashoka ) had a Michelangelo Madonna statute mounted on the top floor. So i took my bike, watched it for about 15 minutes and then came home, with a stiff neck . A lot of people were gaping up from the street along with me wondering what i was looking at-- probably a free , no pantie up-skirt show -- or what? .&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">My mother and child came out exquisite. I used a wire skeleton , and the whole thing just came up like magic. A smaller 1/8 version though. &nbsp;The next day evening i took it to my art teacher.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">He had a look at it , and told me that my statue is too smooth and realistic , and that i must roughen it. He said, art has degenerated , that a smooth statue stood no chance in winning a prize. -- like how a smooth combed male hair do , will be any day beaten by a gel stiffened dishevelled punk Ronaldo hairdo &nbsp;.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-KbPPa7FSn00/TVkSoP8ddXI/AAAAAAAADcQ/pH3_VxdL2a8/s1600/pp.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"400\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-KbPPa7FSn00/TVkSoP8ddXI/AAAAAAAADcQ/pH3_VxdL2a8/s400/pp.jpg\" width=\"343\" /></span></a></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">So in his presence, with a heavy heart, i used a sharp blade and surface chipped the whole thing, and gave it &nbsp;that rough look. The clay was not yet hard. To cut a long story short, it secured the third prize, at All India Level.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Even today I feel, that Michelangelo's masterpiece looks better in the silken smooth NATURAL REALISTIC way.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">It is the age of tattered jeans.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">See the outlandish dresses on FTV on skeleton type females, who cant even walk properly.. They walk funnier than the high steppin' hackneys.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">And for Hollywood award functions see famous actresses shamelessly wear --\" look MA, no yeast on mE twat !\" -- peek a boo gowns, where everything is covered except the crotch. &nbsp;</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Vested magazines and TV critics call the shots.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">My younger son can draw a human face better than me. But there is NO way, he can make a mark in the art world. &nbsp;Like my school art teacher had warned me \" Real art has been hijacked !. It is the era of vested pretenders, who want it a particular way, to achieve their own ends \" .&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-NijqSqXo2Tw/TVkVQkpCmII/AAAAAAAADcU/rzleByUNJfg/s1600/AASHIK+1+001.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"640\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-NijqSqXo2Tw/TVkVQkpCmII/AAAAAAAADcU/rzleByUNJfg/s640/AASHIK+1+001.jpg\" width=\"433\" /></span></a></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-9Pbhyn5aVvE/TVkVZA1ubBI/AAAAAAAADcY/Hdh3076QrZg/s1600/AASHIK+2+001.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"290\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-9Pbhyn5aVvE/TVkVZA1ubBI/AAAAAAAADcY/Hdh3076QrZg/s400/AASHIK+2+001.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></span></a></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"color: blue;\"><i>Let me show 2 paintings of my younger son, which won awards at school, when he was just 9 and 10 years old. &nbsp;He had beaten all 16 year olds.</i></span> &nbsp;<b><span style=\"color: red;\">THE DRAGON PAINTING IS 4D MODERN ART.</span></b></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">I cannot explain degeneration of art, unless I speak about Picasso, the father of modern art.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Indeed Picasso had talent as a young man. But not enough talent to paint your realistic face in 5 minutes. As he grew older, he lost his skills, and others overtook him. Being the shrewd Spaniard he was, he went into abstract , to paint a large mural&nbsp;<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"line-height: 18px;\">11 feet 6 inches high and 25 feet 8 inches wide (3,5 x 7,76 meters) in size. It is shown below.</span></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-Bf9LP0T_99M/TVkXObxh-uI/AAAAAAAADcc/1huEFg-AZnY/s1600/Guernica+-+3.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"304\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-Bf9LP0T_99M/TVkXObxh-uI/AAAAAAAADcc/1huEFg-AZnY/s640/Guernica+-+3.jpg\" width=\"640\" /></span></a></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">In my opinion it was an excellent effort, and he delivered what he was told to do. He showcased the bombing of Guernica, a sleepy small village, in Basque country, by German and Italian warplanes, at the behest of Spanish Nationalist forces on<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"line-height: 17px;\">&nbsp;26 April 1937, during the Spanish civil war. &nbsp;It was&nbsp;</span><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">displayed at the<span class=\"apple-converted-space\">&nbsp;</span>Paris International Exposition in the 1937 World's Fair at Paris.&nbsp;</span></span><br />\n<br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">It now hangs in the Reina Sofia Art Centre madrid.</span></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Two of the world famous comments were--&nbsp;</span></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"></span></span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 4.8pt 0in 6pt;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><i><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">Guernica</span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;shows suffering people, animals, and buildings wrenched by violence and chaos.</span></i></span></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"></span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: 1.2pt; margin-left: 0.25in; mso-list: l1 level1 lfo1; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; tab-stops: list .5in; text-indent: -0.25in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><i><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\u00a7<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;;\">&nbsp; </span></span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">The overall scene is within a room where, at an open end on the left, a wide-eyed bull stands over a woman grieving over a dead child in her arms.</span></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: 1.2pt; margin-left: 0.25in; mso-list: l1 level1 lfo1; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; tab-stops: list .5in; text-indent: -0.25in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><i><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\u00a7<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;;\">&nbsp; </span></span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">The centre is occupied by a horse falling in agony as it had just been run through by a spear or javelin. It is important to note that the large gaping wound in the horse's side is a major focus of the painting.</span></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: 1.2pt; margin-left: 0.25in; mso-list: l1 level1 lfo1; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; tab-stops: list .5in; text-indent: -0.25in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><i><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\u00a7<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;;\">&nbsp; </span></span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">Two \"hidden\" images formed by the horse appear in&nbsp;Guernica:</span></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: 1.2pt; margin-left: 0.5in; mso-list: l1 level2 lfo1; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; tab-stops: list 1.0in; text-indent: -0.25in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><i><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\u00a7<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;;\">&nbsp; </span></span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">A human skull overlays the horse's body.</span></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: 1.2pt; margin-left: 0.5in; mso-list: l1 level2 lfo1; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; tab-stops: list 1.0in; text-indent: -0.25in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><i><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\u00a7<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;;\">&nbsp; </span></span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">A bull appears to gore the horse from underneath. The bull's head is formed mainly by the horse's entire front leg which has the knee on the ground. The leg's knee cap forms the head's nose. A horn appears within the horse's breast.</span></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: 1.2pt; margin-left: 0.25in; mso-list: l1 level1 lfo1; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; tab-stops: list .5in; text-indent: -0.25in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><i><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\u00a7<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;;\">&nbsp; </span></span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">The bull's tail forms the image of a flame with smoke rising from it, seemingly appearing in a window created by the lighter shade of gray surrounding it.</span></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: 1.2pt; margin-left: 0.25in; mso-list: l1 level1 lfo1; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; tab-stops: list .5in; text-indent: -0.25in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><i><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\u00a7<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;;\">&nbsp; </span></span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">Under the horse is a dead, apparently dismembered soldier; his hand on a severed arm still grasps a shattered sword from which a flower grows.</span></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: 1.2pt; margin-left: 0.25in; mso-list: l1 level1 lfo1; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; tab-stops: list .5in; text-indent: -0.25in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><i><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\u00a7<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;;\">&nbsp; </span></span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">On the open palm of the dead soldier is a stigma, a symbol of martyrdom derived from the stigmata</span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;of Christ.</span></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: 1.2pt; margin-left: 0.25in; mso-list: l1 level1 lfo1; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; tab-stops: list .5in; text-indent: -0.25in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><i><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\u00a7<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;;\">&nbsp; </span></span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">A light bulb blazes in the shape of an evil eye over the suffering horse's head (the bare bulb of the torturer's cell.) Picasso's intended symbolism in regards to this object is related to the Spanish word for lightbulb; \"bombilla\", which makes an allusion to \"bomb\" and therefore signifies the destructive effect which technology can have on society.</span></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: 1.2pt; margin-left: 0.25in; mso-list: l1 level1 lfo1; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; tab-stops: list .5in; text-indent: -0.25in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><i><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\u00a7<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;;\">&nbsp; </span></span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">To the upper right of the horse, a frightened female figure, who seems to be witnessing the scenes before her, appears to have floated into the room through a window. Her arm, also floating in, carries a flame-lit lamp. The lamp is positioned very close to the bulb, and is a symbol of hope, clashing with the light bulb.</span></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: 1.2pt; margin-left: 0.25in; mso-list: l1 level1 lfo1; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; tab-stops: list .5in; text-indent: -0.25in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><i><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\u00a7<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;;\">&nbsp; </span></span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">From the right, an awe-struck woman staggers towards the center below the floating female figure. She looks up blankly into the blazing light bulb.</span></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: 1.2pt; margin-left: 0.25in; mso-list: l1 level1 lfo1; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; tab-stops: list .5in; text-indent: -0.25in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><i><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\u00a7<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;;\">&nbsp; </span></span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">Daggers that suggest screaming replace the tongues of the bull, grieving woman, and horse.</span></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: 1.2pt; margin-left: 0.25in; mso-list: l1 level1 lfo1; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; tab-stops: list .5in; text-indent: -0.25in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><i><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\u00a7<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;;\">&nbsp; </span></span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">A bird, possibly a dove, stands on a shelf behind the bull in panic.</span></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: 1.2pt; margin-left: 0.25in; mso-list: l1 level1 lfo1; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; tab-stops: list .5in; text-indent: -0.25in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><i><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\u00a7<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;;\">&nbsp; </span></span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">On the far right, a figure with arms raised in terror is entrapped by fire from above and below.</span></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: 1.2pt; margin-left: 0.25in; mso-list: l1 level1 lfo1; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; tab-stops: list .5in; text-indent: -0.25in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><i><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\u00a7<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;;\">&nbsp; </span></span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">A dark wall with an open door defines the right end of the mural.</span></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: 1.2pt; margin-left: 0.25in; mso-list: l1 level1 lfo1; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; tab-stops: list .5in; text-indent: -0.25in;\">\n<i><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</span></i></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 4.8pt 0in 6pt;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><i><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">BBB ) Made by scholar Beverly Ray</span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">--&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: 1.2pt; margin-left: 0.25in; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo2; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; tab-stops: list .5in; text-indent: -0.25in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><i><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\u00a7<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;;\">&nbsp; </span></span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">The shape and posture of the bodies express protest.</span></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: 1.2pt; margin-left: 0.25in; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo2; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; tab-stops: list .5in; text-indent: -0.25in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><i><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\u00a7<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;;\">&nbsp; </span></span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">Picasso uses black, white, and grey paint to set a somber mood and express pain and chaos.</span></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: 1.2pt; margin-left: 0.25in; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo2; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; tab-stops: list .5in; text-indent: -0.25in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><i><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\u00a7<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;;\">&nbsp; </span></span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">Flaming buildings and crumbling walls not only express the destruction of Guernica, but reflect the destructive power of civil war.</span></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: 1.2pt; margin-left: 0.25in; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo2; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; tab-stops: list .5in; text-indent: -0.25in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><i><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\u00a7<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;;\">&nbsp; </span></span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">The newspaper print used in the painting reflects how Picasso learned of the massacre.</span></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: 1.2pt; margin-left: 0.25in; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo2; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; tab-stops: list .5in; text-indent: -0.25in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><i><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\u00a7<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;;\">&nbsp; </span></span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">The light bulb in the painting represents the sun.</span></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: 1.2pt; margin-left: 0.25in; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo2; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; tab-stops: list .5in; text-indent: -0.25in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><i><span style=\"border: 1pt windowtext; line-height: 150%; padding: 0in;\">\u00a7<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;;\">&nbsp; </span></span></i><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><i>The broken sword near the bottom of the painting symbolizes the defeat of the people at the hand of their tormentors</i>.&nbsp;</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: 1.2pt; margin-left: 0.25in; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo2; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; tab-stops: list .5in; text-indent: -0.25in;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: 1.2pt; margin-left: 0.25in; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo2; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; tab-stops: list .5in; text-indent: -0.25in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">Picasso chipped in -- \"Art is <span style=\"border: 1pt windowtext; padding: 0in;\">a lie that makes us realize truth.&nbsp;</span></span>The symbolism I used includes a dying horse, a woman caught in a burning building, and an anguished mother with a dead child\".</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">It then went around on a world tour, and attracted much applause and comment.&nbsp;</span></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">After this Picasso went into the abstract mode of Cubism. He roped into Cubism &nbsp;Georges Braque, a well known painter.&nbsp;</span></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: red;\"><br />\n</span></span></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: red;\">Cubism came naturally to Picasso ,as he was born a dyslexic</span>.&nbsp;</span></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">He did NOT attend school. His father Jose Ruiz Blasco was an art teacher , and forced him into art, just to make him survive .&nbsp;</span></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Picasso had a very difficult birth on 25th Oct 1881. He became blue , as he did not breathe, as he come out into the world, from the womb. As a last ditch attempt somebody blew a mouthful of heavy cigar smoke into the baby's lungs, causing him to cough and start breathing.</span></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">&nbsp;Later he became a schizophrenic. He took on many wives. Most of them were underage as young as 13. Two of his wives committed suicide and 2 of them went into mental hospitals.</span></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: red; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">They developed a CULT, by striking the right poses and terrific self promotion. &nbsp;If you did not cry WOW-- you were just a moron, who did not understand art, and had no imagination.&nbsp;</span></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Every one were forced to jump into the bandwagon of \" See, the Emperor is wearing clothes!\"</span></span><br />\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 4.8pt 0in 6pt;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"></span></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">The story:&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><i><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue;\">An emperor was approached by two tailors who said that they could make him a suit of clothes of surpassing beauty, and the emperor decided to try them. The tailors asked for hundreds of pounds of thread made of silver and gold, shut themselves up for weeks, and finally came forward with a suit made of cloth so fine that it would be invisible to anyone who was stupid and incompetent. The emperor could not see the suit but he did not want to admit that he was stupid and incompetent, so he decided to put it on.&nbsp;</span></i></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><i><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue;\"><br />\n</span></i></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><i><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue;\">Once they were informed that only those who were not stupid and incompetent could see the suit, all of the emperor's ministers raved about it. The emperor believed that they could see it and was disturbed that he was the only one who was stupid and incompetent. He decided to give a parade so that all of his subjects could admire the new suit.</span></i></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><i><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue;\"><br />\n</span></i></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><i><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue;\">At the parade a little child cried out what all of the spectators saw but were afraid to admit<b>:</b><span class=\"apple-converted-space\">&nbsp;</span>that the emperor was naked, and he could see his balls swinging. The emperor and all the others suddenly realized that the suit did not exist. The tailors were long gone, and of course all the thread of silver and gold that was in the suit.</span></i></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: red; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Picasso founded an art magazine, with rich investors to back him. &nbsp; All made money.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: red;\">The real talented artists were left begging for food.&nbsp;</span></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Cezanne jumped into the bandwagon, crying about the golden rectangle ( ancient Vedic stuff ). Soon Matisse jumped in.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Here is a true event .&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">World famous paintings by the greatest abstract artists, without revealing the name of the artist were displayed. Some of these paintings were hung upside down. A Chimp aged 4 by the name of Congo, had painted several abstract paintings--basically splashed paint. The Chimps work was selected by the world famous, investors , art critics and viewers.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">This just shows how art has been hijacked into a cult, where everybody follows and toes the line , in a zombie manner. These pathetic art critics, absorbed into the cult, &nbsp;love to talk about perception. There is no execution of an idea what-so-ever.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">&nbsp;<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\"><span class=\"apple-style-span\">\"Modernism\" such as cubism and expressionism intentionally distorts and hides reality, it doesn't interpret and explain it, as real art does.</span><span class=\"apple-converted-space\">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 17px;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\"><span class=\"apple-converted-space\"></span></span><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"line-height: 17px;\">We're in the realm of hijacked opinion , not objectivity.&nbsp;</span><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"line-height: 17px;\">Cubism has thrived as an art form and such &nbsp;dreadful daubings are worth many millions.&nbsp;</span></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"line-height: 17px;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-sr7N-oRv_vo/TVkjBa_oPyI/AAAAAAAADcg/BxGVQsoaraQ/s1600/A-cubist-painting.jpeg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; text-align: center;\">\n</div>\n<br /></div>\n<br /></div>\n", "author": {"id": "14410812789424637654", "displayName": "Capt. Ajit Vadakayil", "url": "https://www.blogger.com/profile/14410812789424637654", "image": {"url": "//4.bp.blogspot.com/-QSnd-Z8F7Kc/XFtPudWdwlI/AAAAAAABfq4/vxrkFOO7Iu8Mf6-OaPgw6FPpRDSmMgLdgCK4BGAYYCw/s35/capt%25252BajitC%25252Bvadakayil.JPG"}}, "replies": {"totalItems": "15", "selfLink": "https://www.googleapis.com/blogger/v3/blogs/3564735312144269387/posts/1770823100233095935/comments"}}, {"kind": "blogger#post", "id": "217196469228865050", "blog": {"id": "3564735312144269387"}, "published": "2011-02-13T15:03:00+05:30", "updated": "2011-02-13T15:16:40+05:30", "etag": "\"iHf3yWDE_geBgZ8U7rgZ_xuTeAQ/dGltZXN0YW1wOiAxMjk3NTkwNDAwNDY4Cm9mZnNldDogMTk4MDAwMDAK\"", "url": "http://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.com/2011/02/naive-sailor-radar-anti-collision-capt.html", "selfLink": "https://www.googleapis.com/blogger/v3/blogs/3564735312144269387/posts/217196469228865050", "title": "THE NAIVE SAILOR, RADAR ANTI COLLISION --  CAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL", "content": "<div dir=\"ltr\" style=\"text-align: left;\" trbidi=\"on\"><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-px75nCEv4tw/TVelGEd1guI/AAAAAAAADb4/UclklqBRFFo/s1600/images+%252811%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-px75nCEv4tw/TVelGEd1guI/AAAAAAAADb4/UclklqBRFFo/s1600/images+%252811%2529.jpg\" /></a></div><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-Czs_ePiZFWU/TVelJbB8RII/AAAAAAAADb8/P0ayq04teCQ/s1600/images.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-Czs_ePiZFWU/TVelJbB8RII/AAAAAAAADb8/P0ayq04teCQ/s1600/images.jpg\" /></a></div><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-hZUo0259KuY/TVeoeS9pl4I/AAAAAAAADcI/hAD6Tx0vVi4/s1600/images+%25282%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-hZUo0259KuY/TVeoeS9pl4I/AAAAAAAADcI/hAD6Tx0vVi4/s1600/images+%25282%2529.jpg\" /></a></div><br />\nIn the year 1983, my ship was approaching Tokyo bay.<br />\n<br />\nThe previous 3 days had typhoonic weather, and there would be a mass exodus of all ships and Japanese coasters, eager to reach the next port, or continue fishing, after getting detained for 3 bad weather days.<br />\n<br />\nOn a 12 mile range, in not so good visibility I could see maybe around 300 ships targets. Well we had an ARPA radar, and the OOW had called me up to handle the super dense crazy traffic . In this area, nobody knows ROR. &nbsp;All react like fishermen, unlike the English Channel..<br />\n<br />\nMy third mate continued acquiring targets Ping Ping Ping on the radar, when he should be concentrating on visual mode, with visibility around 2 miles. I told him to change over to RELATIVE trails, as i noticed that he was on true trails mode. I also told him NOT to look further than 6 miles on the radar, cutting down his attention area.<br />\n<br />\nI called up the Radio Officer on bridge and asked him to change the CRT tube of one of the radars with a brand new one, in the spare locker. The old tube had a burnt centre spot and had NIL persistence of vision. <br />\n<br />\nHe did it in a jiffy, and since it was sunset, i could see the good persistence of vision, without the black hood and screen. -- like the modern day TV type radars giving relative trails.<br />\n<br />\nI them told the OOW to put off the ARPA and use only radar mode. Totaly shocked, he told me to repeat my command , thinking he had heard wrong. I again said \" Put off the ARPA, I dont want you to acquire targets on ARPA\".<br />\n<br />\nI took the ship into Yokahama harbour , and then handed over to the pilot. By the time he took over the visibility was around 1 mile.<br />\n<br />\nThe nervous Jap pilot was literally running around like a monkey, peering through the binoculars, frothing from the mouth, bumping here and there, running back to the ARPA and acquiring targets &nbsp;ping , ping, &nbsp;ping all on TRUE vectors. &nbsp; It was a sight to see.<br />\n<br />\nThrice i had to warn the pilot that we were on collision course and make the decision to alter course with pilot on board, whcih is bad protocol , but within maritime law traditions.<br />\n<br />\nMuch later, at port, with cargo work in progress, the OOW ( third mate ) was hanging around my cabin, -- he wanted to speak to me.<br />\n<br />\nHe said : \" Sir, you had hundreds of targets, you were at absolute ease without an ARPA, and made several alterations, which i noticed were all perfect and optimum ones, in such dense traffic, with poor visibility. I am impressed. What was the secret? \"<br />\n<br />\nI said \" Son, it is hard to explain all this to a boy who prefers to wear a digital watch , still i must try\"<br />\n<br />\nHere is the gist--<br />\n<br />\nIf you notice any of your friends , wearing a digital watch, make a mental note that he is NOT TOO BRIGHT. <br />\n<br />\nThis is the way the human brain works. Smarter blokes wear analogue watches, which does not tax the brain. I do not want to digress. That will be another blog.<br />\n<br />\nWe had more than 300 targets on a 12 mile range, all cross traffic, with absolute chaos.<br />\n<br />\nOr say 150 targets forward of beam . Most of the ships had slowed down, and some fishing vessels were stopped..<br />\n<br />\nNow, how many blessed targets could the ARPA acquire? &nbsp;May be about 20 or max 25? ( on that old radar it was just 15 nos )<br />\n<br />\nWhat is the big idea in acquiring 15 out of 150 targets, leaving 135 unacquired? How do you know the 15 you had acquired were actually hostile targets?<br />\n<br />\nEven if you had acquired 15 hostile targets by sheer divine luck, can the human brain take in so much digital information.<br />\n<br />\nHell NO!<br />\n<br />\nNow if you were looking only at the analogue TRUE vectorARPA lines, like what the Jap pilot did, what can you make out of it? &nbsp;Are you interested in knowing the TRUE course and speed of a target? &nbsp;For what?<br />\n<br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: red; font-size: large;\">At sea every target is round. It does NOT have a bow and a stern in bad visibility. It is RELATIVE, RELATIVE, RELATIVE on bridge--</span><br />\n<br />\nWhy did i choose to change the radar CRT tube ?<br />\n<br />\nBecause the persistence of vision afforded gave me RELATIVE trails of all the 300 targets. Any such trail produced in the opposite direction gave me a ready made RELATIVE ARPA vector.<br />\n<br />\nI could instantly see which all targets were hostile. (The reversed relative trails pointing to the radar centre spot )<br />\n<br />\nI could see several targets making crazy emergency alterations of course , by checking out their curving relative trails. I could make out which all fishing targets were stationary, as they gave a parallel trail, of fixed length, based on own ship's speed.<br />\n<br />\nI could see that the ships that did not leave a trail ahead of me were going in the same direction as my ship. I could see who all had slowed down.<br />\n<br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue;\">In fog, if any Navigator or Pilot, uses TRUE vectors on ARPA, only god's grace is saving the ship.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<br />\nThis foolish idiot will think he is in full contraol, while in reality , he is NOT-- he is a most dangerous man to safety of life on baord.<br />\n<br />\nThe only way TRUE ARPA vectors will help, is when you are in a TSS, you would like to know who all are following the TSS scheme as, the ROR is different in TSS. &nbsp;You get to know the true course of the target. Also you can find out which fishing vessel is stopped ( with her nets down/ or sleeping ! )<br />\n<br />\nRELATIVE TRAILS GIVEN BY RADAR PERSISTENCE OF VISION , PRODUCED IN THE OPPOSITE DIRECTION IS SAME AS RELATIVE TRIALS ON ARPA, WITH THE ADVANTAGE THAT YOU DON'T HAVE TO DO PING PING PING, OR BOTHER ABOUT LOST ARPA TARGETS AND ITS ASSOCIATED DISTRACTING ALARMS.<br />\n<br />\nOn modern TV type radars , you have an option of pushing a RELATIVE TRIALS button, and finding out a single hostile target among 150 ahead of you, in one single glance.<br />\n<br />\nThis system is the world's best lookout man, in heavy traffic.<br />\n<br />\nIf you have fed in the timing for the trail length as 3 minutes , all it requires is for a very small boat to come up to the crest of a swell , 3 times in a period of 3 minutes, and it will be pinged.<br />\n<br />\nSo you can ask any OOW, will you have 10 lookout men on each bridge wing, or a nice RELATIVE TRAILS radar screen, which option he would prefer? Only an absolute idiot will say 10 lookout men.<br />\n<br />\nAfter all what will the lookout man tell you? Sir, I can see a light 1 point on port bow--blah--blah-- after a dozen times of this stupid charade, you will go out of your mind, in frustration, for this type misleading information with 150 targets in front, means nothing to you-- right?<br />\n<br />\nAt anchorages , use radar in plotter more, zoomed in, with own ships past TRACK on.. The GPS antenna will leave nice doughnut patterns around your ship's anchor. Even a small shift of 20 metres due to stern yawing will be drawn on the screen. <br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-z-5RZAtwFN4/TVeoU7TgW3I/AAAAAAAADcE/8o2mfwcxxg8/s1600/images+%25281%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-z-5RZAtwFN4/TVeoU7TgW3I/AAAAAAAADcE/8o2mfwcxxg8/s1600/images+%25281%2529.jpg\" /></a></div><br />\nAt sea , you must move with the times.<br />\n<br />\nMorons ashore who do not have an iota of your anti-collision experience will write fancy circulars , and try to brainwash you with his idiotic nonsense. You don't have to accept that.<br />\n<br />\nA week back i did my re validation course , for my Certificate of Competency, and an old ex-captain, with 1/25 of my anti-collision experience was lecturing merrily how to avoid collision with various fancy slides.<br />\n<br />\nBut then sometimes you let it be--<br />\n<br />\n-- we cant take on this crazy world and win in one single day , right? &nbsp; I went there to get a certificate , after being a student for 2 weeks , and i got it! <br />\n<br />\nMission successful!<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-QzpqCEC3n-4/TVeoHvm8v8I/AAAAAAAADcA/17y4YEotAvM/s1600/download.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-QzpqCEC3n-4/TVeoHvm8v8I/AAAAAAAADcA/17y4YEotAvM/s1600/download.jpg\" /></a></div><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow;\">Note: This post is the most valuable of all my Naive series posts.</span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-Y13gR2GCPlg/TVejva9VwhI/AAAAAAAADb0/pkHzuHca2zM/s1600/capt+ajit+vadakayil.JPG\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-Y13gR2GCPlg/TVejva9VwhI/AAAAAAAADb0/pkHzuHca2zM/s1600/capt+ajit+vadakayil.JPG\" /></a></div><br />\nCAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL ( 28 YEARS IN COMMAND )<br />\n..<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n</div>", "author": {"id": "14410812789424637654", "displayName": "Capt.
